------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Bucket index in {0..70}
bucket71 : Nat Рєњ Nat
bucket71 n = n % 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  bucket71-period : Рѕђ n k Рєњ bucket71 (n + k * 71) РЅА bucket71 n
module UFTC_Lattice where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (sym; trans; cong)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (РЅц-refl; РЅц-trans; РЅц-antisym;
  Ріћ-idem; Ріћ-comm; Ріћ-assoc; Ріћ-mono-РЅц; Ріћ-mono╦А-РЅц; Ріћ-mono╩│-РЅц)
open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_; _Ріћ_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Severity levels (0..9). (You can restrict further if you want Fin 10.)

Severity : Set
Severity = Nat

_РіЉ_ : Severity Рєњ Severity Рєњ Set
_РіЉ_ = _РЅц_

-- Join = max severity wins.
_Ріћs_ : Severity Рєњ Severity Рєњ Severity
_Ріћs_ = _Ріћ_

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Join-semilattice laws (assoc/comm/idempotent).

Ріћs-idem : Рѕђ a Рєњ a Ріћs a РЅА a
Ріћs-idem a = NatP.Ріћ-idem a

Ріћs-comm : Рѕђ a b Рєњ a Ріћs b РЅА b Ріћs a
Ріћs-comm a b = NatP.Ріћ-comm a b

Ріћs-assoc : Рѕђ a b c Рєњ (a Ріћs b) Ріћs c РЅА a Ріћs (b Ріћs c)
Ріћs-assoc a b c = NatP.Ріћ-assoc a b c

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Monotonicity of join (the key Рђюmax severity wins cannot be maskedРђЮ).

Ріћs-mono╦А : Рѕђ {a a' b} Рєњ a РіЉ a' Рєњ (a Ріћs b) РіЉ (a' Ріћs b)
Ріћs-mono╦А {a} {a'} {b} aРЅцa' =
  NatP.Ріћ-mono╦А-РЅц b aРЅцa'

Ріћs-mono╩│ : Рѕђ {a b b'} Рєњ b РіЉ b' Рєњ (a Ріћs b) РіЉ (a Ріћs b')
Ріћs-mono╩│ {a} {b} {b'} bРЅцb' =
  NatP.Ріћ-mono╩│-РЅц a bРЅцb'

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A minimal РђюcodeРђЮ model: normal trit + special codes with severity.
-- (Map VOID/PARA/META etc. into severity levels.)

data Code : Set where
  normal : Nat Рєњ Code               -- placeholder for trits
  special : Severity Рєњ Code          -- special failure code with severity

severity : Code Рєњ Severity
severity (normal _)    = 0
severity (special sev) = sev

-- Propagation rule: combine codes by max severity.
C_XOR : Code Рєњ Code Рєњ Code
C_XOR x y = special (severity x Ріћs severity y)

C_ROT : Code Рєњ Code
C_ROT x = x  -- rotation doesn't reduce severity (your fast path can refine)

-- Monotone wrt severity preorder:
MonotoneРѓѓ : (Code Рєњ Code Рєњ Code) Рєњ Set
MonotoneРѓѓ f =
  Рѕђ x x' y y' Рєњ
    severity x РіЉ severity x' Рєњ
    severity y РіЉ severity y' Рєњ
    severity (f x y) РіЉ severity (f x' y')

C_XOR-monotone : MonotoneРѓѓ C_XOR
C_XOR-monotone x x' y y' sx sy =
  NatP.Ріћ-mono-РЅц sx sy

-- Rotation monotonicity (trivial in this stub; replace with your real ROT):
C_ROT-monotone :
  Рѕђ x x' Рєњ severity x РіЉ severity x' Рєњ severity (C_ROT x) РіЉ severity (C_ROT x')
C_ROT-monotone x x' sx = sx

  Рѕђ {D}
  (F : ModelFamily D)

  Рєњ
  (Рѕђ n Рєњ primeTotal (ModelFamily.candidate F k)
          РЅц primeTotal (ModelFamily.candidate F n))
  Рєњ

module MDL where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (Ріц; tt)
open import Data.Empty using (РіЦ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic length type

CodeLength : Set
CodeLength = Nat

_РЅц_ : Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Set
zero РЅц _ = Ріц
suc m РЅц zero = РіЦ
suc m РЅц suc n = m РЅц n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dataset abstraction

record Dataset : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    Data : Set
    sample : Data

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Model abstraction (two-part code)

record Model (D : Dataset) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    Param      : Set
    param      : Param

    encodeM    : Param Рєњ CodeLength
    encodeData : Param Рєњ Dataset.Data D Рєњ CodeLength

modelTotalLength :
  Рѕђ {D} Рєњ
  Model D Рєњ
  CodeLength
modelTotalLength {D} M =
  Model.encodeM M (Model.param M) + Model.encodeData M (Model.param M) (Dataset.sample D)


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- MDL comparison

better :
  Рѕђ {D} Рєњ
  Model D Рєњ
  Model D Рєњ
  Set

better {D} MРѓЂ MРѓѓ =
  modelTotalLength MРѓЂ РЅц modelTotalLength MРѓѓ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Subset selection cost (critical for honesty)

-- Suppose models are parameterized by a subset of primes
-- We must charge for describing that subset.

Subset : Nat Рєњ Set
Subset n = Nat  -- abstract: encoded subset id

subsetCost :
  Рѕђ (n : Nat) Рєњ
  Subset n Рєњ
  CodeLength
subsetCost n _ = n  -- naive upper bound: cost grows with space size

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Bounded model class (limit to 71)

record BoundedModel (D : Dataset) (limit : Nat) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    inner : Model D
    boundProof :
      modelTotalLength inner РЅц limit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The "limit to 71" specialization

limit71 : Nat
limit71 = 71

record Model71 (D : Dataset) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    base : Model D
    bounded : modelTotalLength base РЅц limit71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Theorem: restricting model space does not reduce price unfairly

restrictSafe :
  Рѕђ {D}
  (M : Model D)
  (p : modelTotalLength M РЅц limit71) Рєњ
  modelTotalLength M РЅц limit71

restrictSafe M p = p

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A factor-exponent vector over the 15 primes is a canonical coordinate.

record Vec15 (A : Set) : Set where

  field
    e2  : A; e3  : A; e5  : A; e7  : A; e11 : A
    e13 : A; e17 : A; e19 : A; e23 : A; e29 : A
    e31 : A; e41 : A; e47 : A; e59 : A; e71 : A

postulate
  Text : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- G├Хdel encoding contract:
-- encode gives a Nat; factorMap gives exponents over SSP primes.
-- The key property is that factorMap is a homomorphism for concatenation
-- (or some composition), if you want that. Here we keep it minimal.

postulate
  encode   : Text Рєњ Nat
  factorMap : Text Рєњ FactorVec

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Self-verifying coordinate means: equality of factor-vectors is a stable
-- identifier under the chosen equivalence (you decide what that is).
-- We DO NOT claim it is РђюrealityРђЮ; we claim it is a canonical coordinate.

record CoordinateLaw : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    stable-id :
      Рѕђ (tРѓЂ tРѓѓ : Text) Рєњ
      factorMap tРѓЂ РЅА factorMap tРѓѓ Рєњ encode tРѓЂ РЅА encode tРѓѓ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distinctness

_РЅб_ : Mask Рєњ Mask Рєњ Set
x РЅб y = ┬г (x РЅА y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Contractive on distinct points

record ContractiveРЅб (K : Mask Рєњ Mask) : Set where
  open Ultrametric.Ultrametric UMask
  field
    contractionРЅб : Рѕђ {x y} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ d (K x) (K y) < d x y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Projection to fixed mask is strictly contractive

postulate
  projContractive : Рѕђ target Рєњ ContractiveРЅб (Kernel.K (projectTo target))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point definition

Fixed : (Mask Рєњ Mask) Рєњ Mask Рєњ Set
Fixed K m = K m РЅА m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Unique fixed point for projection

uniqueFixedProj :
  Рѕђ target x y Рєњ
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) x Рєњ
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) y Рєњ
  x РЅА y

module KernelAlgebra where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Base ternary carrier

data T : Set where
  neg  : T
  zero : T
  pos  : T

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- State space as indexed function

State : Set Рєњ Set
State X = X Рєњ T

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution

╬╣ : Рѕђ {X} Рєњ State X Рєњ State X
╬╣ s x with s x
... | neg  = pos
... | pos  = neg
... | zero = zero

╬╣┬▓-id : Рѕђ {X} (s : State X) (x : X) Рєњ ╬╣ (╬╣ s) x РЅА s x
╬╣┬▓-id s x with s x
... | neg  = refl
... | pos  = refl
... | zero = refl


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel operator interface

record Kernel {X : Set} : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    K : State X Рєњ State X

    involutive-respecting :
      Рѕђ s Рєњ K (╬╣ s) РЅА ╬╣ (K s)

open Kernel public

module Stabilisation where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration

iterate : Рѕђ {X} Рєњ
          (State X Рєњ State X) Рєњ
          Nat Рєњ
          State X Рєњ
          State X
iterate K zero    s = s
iterate K (suc n) s = iterate K n (K s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- No nontrivial 2-cycle

No2Cycle : Рѕђ {X} (K : State X Рєњ State X) Рєњ Set
No2Cycle K =
  Рѕђ s Рєњ iterate K 2 s РЅА s Рєњ K s РЅА s
module MonsterStep where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _Рѕи_)

open import MonsterState

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- First admissible candidate (deterministic tie-break: leftmost wins).

choose : (L : Lens) Рєњ (s : State) Рєњ Candidates Рєњ Mask Рєњ Mask
choose L s []           fallback = fallback
choose L s (m Рѕи ms)     fallback with Lens.admissible L s m
... | true  = m
... | false = choose L s ms fallback

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Step:
-- - pick next mask via lens
-- - advance window (or keep it; you decide)
-- This pins MW-00 (well-defined deterministic function).

step : (L : Lens) Рєњ Candidates Рєњ State Рєњ State
step L cands s =
  let nextMask = choose L s cands (State.mask s)
  in  st nextMask (suc (State.window s))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration (total, structurally terminating on Nat).

iterate : Рѕђ {A : Set} Рєњ (A Рєњ A) Рєњ Nat Рєњ A Рєњ A
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)
module Contraction where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Data.Empty using (РіЦ)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Contraction property (strict)

_РЅб_ : Рѕђ {A : Set} Рєњ A Рєњ A Рєњ Set
x РЅб y = x РЅА y Рєњ РіЦ

record Contractive
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S Рєњ S)
       : Set where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U

  field
    contraction :
      Рѕђ x y Рєњ
      d (K x) (K y) < d x y

-- Contractive on distinct points (avoids x=x degenerate case).
record ContractiveРЅб
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S Рєњ S)
       : Set where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U

  field
    contractionРЅб :
      Рѕђ {x y} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ
      d (K x) (K y) < d x y

-- Strict contraction plus a specified unique fixed point.
record StrictContraction
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S Рєњ S)
       : Set where

  field
    contractiveРЅб : ContractiveРЅб U K
    fp : S
    fixed : K fp РЅА fp
    unique : Рѕђ x Рєњ K x РЅА x Рєњ x РЅА fp
module MonsterMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- We model the 15 prime-power factors of |M| as positions 0..14.

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A mask is a length-15 boolean list:
-- true  = keep factor
-- false = remove factor

Mask : Set
Mask = List Bool

replicate : Nat Рєњ Bool Рєњ Mask
replicate zero    b = []
replicate (suc n) b = b Рѕи replicate n b

boolAnd : Bool Рєњ Bool Рєњ Bool
boolAnd true true = true
boolAnd _    _    = false

notBool : Bool Рєњ Bool
notBool true  = false
notBool false = true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonical full mask (all factors kept)

fullMask : Mask
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Collapse mask: remove everything

emptyMask : Mask
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Pointwise AND (factor removal composition)

_РѕД_ : Mask Рєњ Mask Рєњ Mask
[] РѕД [] = []
(b Рѕи xs) РѕД (c Рѕи ys) = boolAnd b c Рѕи (xs РѕД ys)
_ РѕД _ = []

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel-style operator: remove a fixed subset F

record Kernel : Set where
  field
    K : Mask Рєњ Mask

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Example: projection to a fixed group representative mask

projectTo : Mask Рєњ Kernel
projectTo target = record
  { K = ╬╗ _ Рєњ target
  }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution: flip keep/remove

flipMask : Mask Рєњ Mask
flipMask [] = []
flipMask (b Рѕи xs) = notBool b Рѕи flipMask xs

module MonsterOntos where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong)
open import Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core using (Dec; yes; no)
open import Data.Nat.Properties renaming (_РЅЪ_ to natРЅЪ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ontos: the 15 supersingular primes used as the base carrier.

data SSP : Set where
  p2  : SSP
  p3  : SSP
  p5  : SSP
  p7  : SSP
  p11 : SSP
  p13 : SSP
  p17 : SSP
  p19 : SSP
  p23 : SSP
  p29 : SSP
  p31 : SSP
  p41 : SSP
  p47 : SSP
  p59 : SSP
  p71 : SSP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete embedding to Nat (for mod/sharding etc).

toNat : SSP Рєњ Nat
toNat p2  = 2
toNat p3  = 3
toNat p5  = 5
toNat p7  = 7
toNat p11 = 11
toNat p13 = 13
toNat p17 = 17
toNat p19 = 19
toNat p23 = 23
toNat p29 = 29
toNat p31 = 31
toNat p41 = 41
toNat p47 = 47
toNat p59 = 59
toNat p71 = 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- toNat is injective because each prime maps to a unique Nat

toNat-injective : Рѕђ {p q} Рєњ toNat p РЅА toNat q Рєњ p РЅА q
toNat-injective {p = p2}  {q = p2}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p3}  {q = p3}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p5}  {q = p5}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p7}  {q = p7}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p11} {q = p11} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p13} {q = p13} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p17} {q = p17} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p19} {q = p19} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p23} {q = p23} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p29} {q = p29} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p31} {q = p31} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p41} {q = p41} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p47} {q = p47} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p59} {q = p59} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p71} {q = p71} refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decide equality by comparing the embedded Nat values

_РЅЪ_ : (p q : SSP) Рєњ Dec (p РЅА q)
_РЅЪ_ p q with natРЅЪ (toNat p) (toNat q)
... | yes eq   = yes (toNat-injective eq)
... | no contra = no (╬╗ eq Рєњ contra (cong toNat eq))

    closed :
      Рѕђ (f g : Endo {X}) Рєњ Endo {X}
module SWAR_Equivalence where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (cong; congРѓѓ; sym; trans)

open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using ()

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lane-wise reference operation:
laneXOR : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Code n Рєњ Vec Code n Рєњ Vec Code n
laneXOR = zipWith C_XOR

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract packed SWAR representation + pack/unpack:
postulate
  Packed : Nat Рєњ Set
  pack   : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Code n Рєњ Packed n
  unpack : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Packed n Рєњ Vec Code n

-- Packed operation (your SWAR fast-path):
postulate
  swarXOR : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Packed n Рєњ Packed n Рєњ Packed n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The *only* thing you need to trust SWAR: a bisimulation/refinement law.

record SWARCorrect : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    -- pack/unpack are section/retraction on the domain you care about
    unpack-pack : Рѕђ {n} (v : Vec Code n) Рєњ unpack (pack v) РЅА v

    -- swarXOR refines laneXOR through unpack
    swar-sound :
      Рѕђ {n} (x y : Packed n) Рєњ
        unpack (swarXOR x y) РЅА laneXOR (unpack x) (unpack y)

-- Derived: swarXOR correct on packed values built from vectors
swar-correct-on-packed :
  (C : SWARCorrect) Рєњ
  Рѕђ {n} (vx vy : Vec Code n) Рєњ
    unpack (swarXOR (pack vx) (pack vy)) РЅА laneXOR vx vy
swar-correct-on-packed C vx vy =
  let open SWARCorrect C in
  trans (swar-sound (pack vx) (pack vy))
        (congРѓѓ laneXOR (unpack-pack vx) (unpack-pack vy))
module PrimeSubsetModel where

open import MDL
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract prime index

PrimeIndex : Set
PrimeIndex = Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- General subset model

record PrimeModel (D : Dataset) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    subsetSize : Nat
    subsetId   : Subset subsetSize
    baseModel  : Model D

primeTotal :
  Рѕђ {D} Рєњ
  PrimeModel D Рєњ
  CodeLength
primeTotal {D} M =
  subsetCost (PrimeModel.subsetSize M) (PrimeModel.subsetId M)
    + modelTotalLength (PrimeModel.baseModel M)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 71-restricted version

record PrimeModel71 (D : Dataset) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    base : PrimeModel D
    sizeBound : PrimeModel.subsetSize base РЅц 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Safety theorem

subsetBoundedCost :
  Рѕђ {D}
  (M : PrimeModel71 D) Рєњ
  PrimeModel.subsetSize (PrimeModel71.base M) РЅц 71

subsetBoundedCost M =
  PrimeModel71.sizeBound M

module Base369 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Utility: repeated rotation
------------------------------------------------------------------------

spin : {A : Set} Рєњ Nat Рєњ (A Рєњ A) Рєњ A Рєњ A
spin 0       rot x = x
spin (suc n) rot x = rot (spin n rot x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Truth values
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data TriTruth : Set where
  tri-low  : TriTruth
  tri-mid  : TriTruth
  tri-high : TriTruth

tri-index : TriTruth Рєњ Nat
tri-index tri-low  = 0
tri-index tri-mid  = 1
tri-index tri-high = 2

rotateTri : TriTruth Рєњ TriTruth
rotateTri tri-low  = tri-mid
rotateTri tri-mid  = tri-high
rotateTri tri-high = tri-low

triXor : TriTruth Рєњ TriTruth Рєњ TriTruth
triXor carrier target = spin (tri-index carrier) rotateTri target

rotateTri┬│ : Рѕђ t Рєњ rotateTri (rotateTri (rotateTri t)) РЅА t
rotateTri┬│ tri-low  = refl
rotateTri┬│ tri-mid  = refl
rotateTri┬│ tri-high = refl

triXor-identity╦А : Рѕђ t Рєњ triXor tri-low t РЅА t
triXor-identity╦А _ = refl

triXor-assoc : Рѕђ a b c Рєњ triXor a (triXor b c) РЅА triXor (triXor a b) c
triXor-assoc tri-low  _        _ = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-low  c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-mid  c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-high c rewrite rotateTri┬│ c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-low  c rewrite rotateTri┬│ c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-mid  c rewrite rotateTri┬│ c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-high c rewrite rotateTri┬│ c = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- A hexadic universe: six РђюbeatsРђЮ that wrap around.

data HexTruth : Set where
  hex-0 hex-1 hex-2 hex-3 hex-4 hex-5 : HexTruth

hex-index : HexTruth Рєњ Nat
hex-index hex-0 = 0
hex-index hex-1 = 1
hex-index hex-2 = 2
hex-index hex-3 = 3
hex-index hex-4 = 4
hex-index hex-5 = 5

rotateHex : HexTruth Рєњ HexTruth
rotateHex hex-0 = hex-1
rotateHex hex-1 = hex-2
rotateHex hex-2 = hex-3
rotateHex hex-3 = hex-4
rotateHex hex-4 = hex-5
rotateHex hex-5 = hex-0

hexXor : HexTruth Рєњ HexTruth Рєњ HexTruth
hexXor carrier target = spin (hex-index carrier) rotateHex target

rotateHexРЂХ : Рѕђ h Рєњ spin 6 rotateHex h РЅА h
rotateHexРЂХ hex-0 = refl
rotateHexРЂХ hex-1 = refl
rotateHexРЂХ hex-2 = refl
rotateHexРЂХ hex-3 = refl
rotateHexРЂХ hex-4 = refl
rotateHexРЂХ hex-5 = refl

hexXor-identity╦А : Рѕђ h Рєњ hexXor hex-0 h РЅА h
hexXor-identity╦А _ = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- A nonary universe: nine РђюvoxelsРђЮ in a ring.

data NonaryTruth : Set where
  non-0 non-1 non-2 non-3 non-4 non-5 non-6 non-7 non-8 : NonaryTruth

nonary-index : NonaryTruth Рєњ Nat
nonary-index non-0 = 0
nonary-index non-1 = 1
nonary-index non-2 = 2
nonary-index non-3 = 3
nonary-index non-4 = 4
nonary-index non-5 = 5
nonary-index non-6 = 6
nonary-index non-7 = 7
nonary-index non-8 = 8

rotateNonary : NonaryTruth Рєњ NonaryTruth
rotateNonary non-0 = non-1
rotateNonary non-1 = non-2
rotateNonary non-2 = non-3
rotateNonary non-3 = non-4
rotateNonary non-4 = non-5
rotateNonary non-5 = non-6
rotateNonary non-6 = non-7
rotateNonary non-7 = non-8
rotateNonary non-8 = non-0

nonaryXor : NonaryTruth Рєњ NonaryTruth Рєњ NonaryTruth
nonaryXor carrier target = spin (nonary-index carrier) rotateNonary target

rotateNonaryРЂ╣ : Рѕђ n Рєњ spin 9 rotateNonary n РЅА n
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-0 = refl
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-1 = refl
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-2 = refl
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-3 = refl
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-4 = refl
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-5 = refl
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-6 = refl
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-7 = refl
rotateNonaryРЂ╣ non-8 = refl

nonaryXor-identity╦А : Рѕђ n Рєњ nonaryXor non-0 n РЅА n
nonaryXor-identity╦А _ = refl
module HeckeScan where

open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)

open import MonsterOntos

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A computational/cognitive state.
postulate
  State : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Hecke operator family: T_p : State Рєњ State for each p in the ontos.

record HeckeFamily : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    T : SSP Рєњ State Рєњ State

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A "compatibility detector" is just a predicate you choose.
-- Example: does the state remain invariant under T_p?

Compat : HeckeFamily Рєњ SSP Рєњ State Рєњ Bool
Compat H p s = true  -- placeholder; define concretely in your pipeline

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A scan produces a 15-bit signature (compatibility bits across primes).

record Sig15 : Set where
  constructor sig15
  field
    b2  : Bool; b3  : Bool; b5  : Bool; b7  : Bool; b11 : Bool
    b13 : Bool; b17 : Bool; b19 : Bool; b23 : Bool; b29 : Bool
    b31 : Bool; b41 : Bool; b47 : Bool; b59 : Bool; b71 : Bool

scan : HeckeFamily Рєњ State Рєњ Sig15
scan H s = sig15
  (Compat H p2  s) (Compat H p3  s) (Compat H p5  s) (Compat H p7  s) (Compat H p11 s)
  (Compat H p13 s) (Compat H p17 s) (Compat H p19 s) (Compat H p23 s) (Compat H p29 s)
  (Compat H p31 s) (Compat H p41 s) (Compat H p47 s) (Compat H p59 s) (Compat H p71 s)

  { K = ╬╗ s Рєњ s
  ; involutive-respecting = ╬╗ s Рєњ refl
  }

-- Another concrete kernel: pointwise involution.

  { K = ╬╣
  ; involutive-respecting = ╬╗ s Рєњ refl
  }

K-neg2-pointwise : Рѕђ {X : Set} (s : State X) (x : X) Рєњ
  Kernel.K (K-neg {X}) (Kernel.K (K-neg {X}) s) x РЅА s x

module MonsterUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List
open import Data.Nat as Nat using (_<_; _РЅц_; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

open import Ultrametric
open import MonsterMask

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distance = index of first differing bit (or 0 if identical)

firstDiff : Mask Рєњ Mask Рєњ Nat Рєњ Nat
firstDiff [] [] _ = 0
firstDiff (true  Рѕи xs) (true  Рѕи ys) n = firstDiff xs ys (suc n)
firstDiff (false Рѕи xs) (false Рѕи ys) n = firstDiff xs ys (suc n)
firstDiff _ _ n = n

dMask : Mask Рєњ Mask Рєњ Nat
dMask x y = firstDiff x y 0

firstDiff-self-zero : Рѕђ m n Рєњ firstDiff m m n РЅА 0
firstDiff-self-zero [] n = refl
firstDiff-self-zero (true Рѕи xs) n = firstDiff-self-zero xs (suc n)
firstDiff-self-zero (false Рѕи xs) n = firstDiff-self-zero xs (suc n)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Identity distance

id-zeroMask : Рѕђ m Рєњ dMask m m РЅА 0
id-zeroMask m = firstDiff-self-zero m 0

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Symmetry

postulate
  symMask : Рѕђ x y Рєњ dMask x y РЅА dMask y x
  ultraMask : Рѕђ x y z Рєњ dMask x z РЅц max (dMask x y) (dMask y z)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

UMask : Ultrametric Mask
UMask = record
  { d            = dMask
  ; id-zero      = id-zeroMask
  ; symmetric    = symMask
  ; ultratriangle = ultraMask
  }
module MonsterSpec where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List)

open import MonsterState
open import MonsterStep

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonical spec = step + optional encoding function.

record Spec : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    L     : Lens
    cands : Candidates

  stepSpec : State Рєњ State
  stepSpec = step L cands

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Optional: a G├Хdel-style encoding of state Рєњ Nat (placeholder).
-- Keep it separate: encoding is a different layer from stepping.

postulate
  encode : State Рєњ Nat
  decode : Nat Рєњ State

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The canonical property youРђЎll ultimately want:
-- decode (encode s) РЅА s  (and/or encode Рѕў decode id on a domain)
module HGSA_Fixpoints where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat.Base using (_<_ )
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Verification.Prelude using (РіЦ; Ріц; tt; ╬Б; _,_; _├Ќ_; ┬г_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (trans; cong)
open import Data.Sum.Base using (_Ріј_; injРѓЂ; injРѓѓ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract state machine for HGSA
postulate
  State : Set
  step  : State Рєњ State

-- Observable predicates
postulate
  Safe   : State Рєњ Set
  Ascend : State Рєњ Set   -- Рђюthis step is an ascend eventРђЮ (or state tagged)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Least fixpoint style РђюEventuallyРђЮ (inductive)
data Eventually (P : State Рєњ Set) : State Рєњ Set where
  now  : Рѕђ {s} Рєњ P s Рєњ Eventually P s
  later : Рѕђ {s} Рєњ Eventually P (step s) Рєњ Eventually P s

-- AlwaysEventuallySafe: eventually Safe OR Ascend
AES : State Рєњ Set
AES s = Eventually (╬╗ t Рєњ Safe t Ріј Ascend t) s

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ranking-function obligation: progress unless already Safe/Ascend.
postulate
  rank : State Рєњ Nat
  progress :
    Рѕђ s Рєњ (┬г Safe s) Рєњ (┬г Ascend s) Рєњ rank (step s) < rank s

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Termination/liveness proof from rank (standard well-founded descent)
-- In Nat, strict descent implies cannot continue forever without hitting base.

postulate
  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    Рѕђ (r : State Рєњ Nat) (f : State Рєњ State) Рєњ
    (Рѕђ s Рєњ r (f s) < r s) Рєњ РіЦ

-- Practical AES theorem: Either Safe/Ascend holds now, or progress gives later.
postulate
  decideSafe : Рѕђ s Рєњ (Safe s Ріј ┬г Safe s)
  decideAsc  : Рѕђ s Рєњ (Ascend s Ріј ┬г Ascend s)

{-# NON_TERMINATING #-}
AES-theorem : Рѕђ s Рєњ AES s
AES-theorem s with decideSafe s | decideAsc s
... | injРѓЂ safeNow | _          = now (injРѓЂ safeNow)
... | injРѓѓ ns      | injРѓЂ ascNow = now (injРѓѓ ascNow)
... | injРѓѓ ns      | injРѓѓ na     =
    later (AES-theorem (step s))
module Overflow where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat ; zero ; suc)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Local congruence lemma (no stdlib needed)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

congOverflow : Рѕђ {A B : Set} {x y : A} (f : A Рєњ B) Рєњ x РЅА y Рєњ f x РЅА f y
congOverflow f refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic relations on РёЋ (custom strict order)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

infix 4 _РЅ║_

data _РЅ║_ : Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Set where
  zРЅ║s : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ zero РЅ║ suc n
  sРЅ║s : Рѕђ {m n} Рєњ m РЅ║ n Рєњ suc m РЅ║ suc n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Voxel states
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Voxel : Set where
  grounded plateau ascended : Voxel

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Threshold guards with explicit proofs
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- Each constructor carries the witness required to justify the
-- classification relative to the threshold.
data VoxelGuard (threshold value : Nat) : Set where
  stay   : value РЅ║ threshold Рєњ VoxelGuard threshold value
  pivot  : threshold РЅА value Рєњ VoxelGuard threshold value
  ascend : threshold РЅ║ value Рєњ VoxelGuard threshold value

state : Рѕђ {t v} Рєњ VoxelGuard t v Рєњ Voxel
state (stay _)   = grounded
state (pivot _)  = plateau
state (ascend _) = ascended

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helper: deterministically choose a guard by structural comparison
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Order : Set where below equal above : Order

compare : Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Order
compare zero    zero    = equal
compare zero    (suc _) = below
compare (suc _) zero    = above
compare (suc a) (suc b) = compare a b

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Relations exposed by comparison tokens
------------------------------------------------------------------------

compare-belowРєњРЅ║ : Рѕђ {t v} Рєњ compare t v РЅА below Рєњ t РЅ║ v
compare-belowРєњРЅ║ {zero}   {zero}   ()
compare-belowРєњРЅ║ {zero}   {suc _}  refl = zРЅ║s
compare-belowРєњРЅ║ {suc _}  {zero}   ()
compare-belowРєњРЅ║ {suc t}  {suc v}  pr   = sРЅ║s (compare-belowРєњРЅ║ {t} {v} pr)

compare-aboveРєњРЅ║ : Рѕђ {t v} Рєњ compare t v РЅА above Рєњ v РЅ║ t
compare-aboveРєњРЅ║ {zero}   {zero}   ()
compare-aboveРєњРЅ║ {zero}   {suc _}  ()
compare-aboveРєњРЅ║ {suc _}  {zero}   refl = zРЅ║s
compare-aboveРєњРЅ║ {suc t}  {suc v}  pr   = sРЅ║s (compare-aboveРєњРЅ║ {t} {v} pr)

compare-equalРєњРЅА : Рѕђ {t v} Рєњ compare t v РЅА equal Рєњ t РЅА v
compare-equalРєњРЅА {zero}  {zero}  refl = refl
compare-equalРєњРЅА {zero}  {suc _} ()
compare-equalРєњРЅА {suc _} {zero} ()
compare-equalРєњРЅА {suc t} {suc v} pr = congOverflow suc (compare-equalРєњРЅА {t} {v} pr)

compare-РЅ║Рєњbelow : Рѕђ {t v} Рєњ t РЅ║ v Рєњ compare t v РЅА below
compare-РЅ║Рєњbelow zРЅ║s      = refl
compare-РЅ║Рєњbelow (sРЅ║s p)  = compare-РЅ║Рєњbelow p

compare-roundtrip-below : Рѕђ {t v} (p : t РЅ║ v) Рєњ compare-belowРєњРЅ║ (compare-РЅ║Рєњbelow p) РЅА p
compare-roundtrip-below zРЅ║s      = refl
compare-roundtrip-below (sРЅ║s p)  = congOverflow sРЅ║s (compare-roundtrip-below p)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enforcement by comparison
------------------------------------------------------------------------


open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_РЅА_; refl)

enforce : (threshold value : Nat) Рєњ VoxelGuard threshold value
enforce zero    zero    = pivot refl
enforce zero    (suc v) = ascend zРЅ║s
enforce (suc t) zero    = stay zРЅ║s
enforce (suc t) (suc v) with enforce t v
... | stay p   = stay   (sРЅ║s p)
... | pivot p  = pivot  (congOverflow suc p)
... | ascend p = ascend (sРЅ║s p)


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Correctness of enforcement
------------------------------------------------------------------------

enforce-ascended-if : Рѕђ {t v} (p : t РЅ║ v) Рєњ enforce t v РЅА ascend p
enforce-ascended-if {zero}  {suc v} zРЅ║s = refl
enforce-ascended-if {suc t} {suc v} (sРЅ║s p) rewrite enforce-ascended-if {t} {v} p = refl

only-if : Рѕђ {t v} Рєњ state (enforce t v) РЅА ascended Рєњ t РЅ║ v
only-if {t} {v} with enforce t v
... | stay   _ = ╬╗ ()
... | pivot  _ = ╬╗ ()
... | ascend p = ╬╗ _ Рєњ p

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Extra comparison lemmas (if you still want them)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

compare-eq-below : Рѕђ {t v} Рєњ compare t v РЅА below Рєњ t РЅ║ v
compare-eq-below {zero}    {zero}    ()
compare-eq-below {zero}    {suc _}   refl = zРЅ║s
compare-eq-below {suc _}   {zero}    ()
compare-eq-below {suc t}   {suc v}   p = sРЅ║s (compare-eq-below {t} {v} p)

compare-eq-above : Рѕђ {t v} Рєњ compare t v РЅА above Рєњ v РЅ║ t
compare-eq-above {zero}    {zero}    ()
compare-eq-above {zero}    {suc _}   ()
compare-eq-above {suc _}   {zero}    refl = zРЅ║s
compare-eq-above {suc t}   {suc v}   p = sРЅ║s (compare-eq-above {t} {v} p)

module DASHI.Geometry.NatNoInfiniteDescent where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_)
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_)
open import Data.Empty            using (РіЦ; РіЦ-elim)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong)

iterate : Рѕђ {S : Set} Рєњ (S Рєњ S) Рєњ Nat Рєњ S Рєњ S
iterate f zero    s = s
iterate f (suc n) s = iterate f n (f s)

-- No infinite strict descent on Nat:
-- If H(f s) < H s for all s, then starting from sРѓђ you get an infinite
-- descending chain in Nat, which contradicts accessibility.
postulate
  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    Рѕђ {S : Set} (H : S Рєњ Nat) (f : S Рєњ S) (sРѓђ : S) Рєњ
    (Рѕђ s Рєњ H (f s) < H s) Рєњ РіЦ
module DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeedInstanceShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift as ROSS
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

-- Fixed locality radius (nontrivial, but simple).
radius : Nat
radius = suc zero

local : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ Set
local {n} x y = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y РЅц radius

preservesLocality :
  Рѕђ {m k} (x y : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  local x y Рєњ
  local (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
        (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)))
preservesLocality {m} {k} x y h =
  let
    open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    step1 : d (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)) (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
            РЅц d (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)
    step1 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpP {m} {k}) (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)
    step2 : d (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y) РЅц d x y
    step2 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpR {m} {k}) x y
    step3 : d (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
               (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)))
            РЅц d (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
               (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
    step3 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpC {m} {k})
              (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
              (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
  in
  NatP.РЅц-trans (NatP.РЅц-trans step3 step1) (NatP.РЅц-trans step2 h)

realFiniteSpeedInstance :
  Рѕђ {m k} Рєњ
  RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (╬╗ x Рєњ ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realFiniteSpeedInstance {m} {k} =
  record
    { local = local {n = m + k}
    ; preservesLocality = preservesLocality {m} {k}
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.Signature31AndDim3 where

record LorentzData : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    QuadraticForm : Set
    Signature : Set
    sig31 : Signature

    Cone : Set

  field
    isotropy : Рѕђ (Q : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) Рєњ Set
    finiteSpeed : Рѕђ (Q : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) Рєњ Set
    convex : Рѕђ (Q : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) Рєњ Set

      Рѕђ (Q Q' : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) Рєњ

  finiteSpeed A Q Рєњ
  convex A Q Рєњ
  nondeg A Q Рєњ

  SignatureUniqueness A Рєњ
  Dim3Witness D Рєњ
  LorentzDimClosure A
mkLorentzDimClosure A sigPf dimPf =
  record { sigProof = sigPf ; dimProof = dimPf }
module DASHI.Geometry.NoStrictDescentForInvertible where

record InvertibleNat (S : Set) : Set where
  field
    step  : S Рєњ S
    inv   : S Рєњ S
    left  : Рѕђ s Рєњ inv (step s) РЅА s
    right : Рѕђ s Рєњ step (inv s) РЅА s
    H     : S Рєњ Nat

-- Invertible step implies you can Рђюwalk backwards foreverРђЮ,
-- contradicting strict descent everywhere.
invertible-no-strict-descent :
  Рѕђ {S} (U : InvertibleNat S) Рєњ
  (sРѓђ : S) Рєњ
  ┬г (Рѕђ s Рєњ InvertibleNat.H U (InvertibleNat.step U s) < InvertibleNat.H U s)
invertible-no-strict-descent U sРѓђ strict =
  NatNoInfiniteDescent (InvertibleNat.H U) (InvertibleNat.step U) sРѓђ strict

record BianchiBundle (geometry : Geometry) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    matter : Matter (Geometry.M geometry)
    first : Рѕђ x y z Рєњ Geometry.BianchiFirst geometry x y z
    second : Рѕђ x y z Рєњ Geometry.BianchiSecond geometry x y z

      Рѕђ x y Рєњ Geometry.G╬╝╬й geometry x y РЅА Matter.T╬╝╬й matter x y

  Рєњ (bundle : BianchiBundle geometry)

    { first = BianchiBundle.first bundle

module DASHI.Geometry.NoLeakageOrthogonality where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Inner-product data supplied as assumptions (no metas/stubs).
----------------------------------------------------------------

record InnerProductData : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    V : Set
    _+_ _-_ _*_ : V Рєњ V Рєњ V
    0v : V
    two : V
    РЪф_,_РЪФ : V Рєњ V Рєњ V
    РѕЦ_РѕЦ┬▓ : V Рєњ V
    add-norm┬▓ :
      Рѕђ a b Рєњ РѕЦ a + b РѕЦ┬▓ РЅА (РѕЦ a РѕЦ┬▓ + РѕЦ b РѕЦ┬▓) + (two * РЪф a , b РЪФ)
    cancel-add-left : Рѕђ {a c} Рєњ a РЅА a + c Рєњ c РЅА 0v
    div2-zero : Рѕђ {z} Рєњ two * z РЅА 0v Рєњ z РЅА 0v

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Projections and Рђюno leakage РЄњ orthogonalityРђЮ
----------------------------------------------------------------

record Projection (D : InnerProductData) : SetРѓЂ where
  open InnerProductData D
  field
    P : V Рєњ V
    idem : Рѕђ x Рєњ P (P x) РЅА P x
    split : Рѕђ x Рєњ P x + (x - P x) РЅА x

coarse : Рѕђ {D} Рєњ Projection D Рєњ InnerProductData.V D Рєњ InnerProductData.V D
coarse Pr x = Projection.P Pr x

detail : Рѕђ {D} Рєњ Projection D Рєњ InnerProductData.V D Рєњ InnerProductData.V D
detail {D} Pr x =
  let open InnerProductData D in x - Projection.P Pr x

NoLeakage : Рѕђ {D} Рєњ Projection D Рєњ Set
NoLeakage {D} Pr =
  Рѕђ x Рєњ РѕЦ x РѕЦ┬▓ РЅА РѕЦ coarse Pr x РѕЦ┬▓ + РѕЦ detail Pr x РѕЦ┬▓
  where open InnerProductData D

Orthogonal : Рѕђ {D} Рєњ Projection D Рєњ Set
Orthogonal {D} Pr =
  Рѕђ x Рєњ РЪф coarse Pr x , detail Pr x РЪФ РЅА 0v
  where open InnerProductData D

NoLeakageРЄњOrthogonal :
  Рѕђ {D} (Pr : Projection D) Рєњ
  NoLeakage Pr Рєњ
  Orthogonal Pr
NoLeakageРЄњOrthogonal {D} Pr NL x =
  let open Projection Pr
      open InnerProductData D
      c = coarse Pr x
      d = detail Pr x
      eq1 = NL x
      eq2 = add-norm┬▓ c d
      eqSplit = sym (cong (╬╗ z Рєњ РѕЦ z РѕЦ┬▓) (split x))
      eq2' = trans eqSplit eq2
      eq3 = trans (sym eq1) eq2'
  in
  div2-zero (cancel-add-left eq3)

module DASHI.Geometry.ParallelogramToInnerProduct where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (╬Б; _,_)
open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_)

postulate
  V : Set
  _+_ _-_ : V Рєњ V Рєњ V
  0v : V

  Рёџ : Set
  _+q_ _-q_ _*q_ : Рёџ Рєњ Рёџ Рєњ Рёџ
  inv2 inv4 : Рёџ

  РѕЦ_РѕЦ┬▓ : V Рєњ Рёџ

Parallelogram : Set
Parallelogram =
  Рѕђ x y Рєњ
    РѕЦ (x + y) РѕЦ┬▓ +q РѕЦ (x - y) РѕЦ┬▓ РЅА
    (inv2 *q ((РѕЦ x РѕЦ┬▓ +q РѕЦ x РѕЦ┬▓) +q (РѕЦ y РѕЦ┬▓ +q РѕЦ y РѕЦ┬▓)))

polarization : V Рєњ V Рєњ Рёџ
polarization x y =
  inv4 *q (РѕЦ (x + y) РѕЦ┬▓ -q РѕЦ (x - y) РѕЦ┬▓)

record InnerProduct : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    ip : V Рєњ V Рєњ Рёџ

ParallelogramРЄњInnerProduct :
  Parallelogram Рєњ
  InnerProduct
ParallelogramРЄњInnerProduct _ = record { ip = polarization }

-- The polarization identity is captured by `ip`, enabling downstream use of the quadratic form.
module DASHI.Geometry.FixedPointExistence_Projection where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (trans; sym)

open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 using (Mask15; Kernel; projectTo)
open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterUltrametric15 using (UMask15)
open import Ultrametric

Fixed : (Mask15 Рєњ Mask15) Рєњ Mask15 Рєњ Set
Fixed K m = K m РЅА m

iterate : (Mask15 Рєњ Mask15) Рєњ Nat Рєњ Mask15 Рєњ Mask15
iterate K zero    m = m
iterate K (suc n) m = iterate K n (K m)

-- For projection K = ╬╗ _ Рєњ target:
-- (1) target is a fixed point
fixed-target : Рѕђ target Рєњ Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) target
fixed-target target = refl

-- (2) unique fixed point
unique-fixed :
  Рѕђ target x y Рєњ
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) x Рєњ
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) y Рєњ
  x РЅА y
unique-fixed target x y fx fy = trans (sym fx) fy

-- (3) convergence in 1 step
converges-1 :
  Рѕђ target m Рєњ iterate (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) 1 m РЅА target
converges-1 target m = refl
module DASHI.Geometry.FiniteSpeed where

open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (Ріц; tt)

record FiniteSpeed {S : Set} (T : S Рєњ S) : SetРѓЂ where

    preservesLocality :
      Рѕђ x y Рєњ local x y Рєњ local (T x) (T y)

-- Trivial finite-speed: all points are local, preserved by any T.
trivialFiniteSpeed :
  Рѕђ {S : Set} (T : S Рєњ S) Рєњ

    { local = ╬╗ _ _ Рєњ Ріц
    ; preservesLocality = ╬╗ _ _ _ Рєњ tt
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.ContractiveDemo where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Nullary      using (┬г_; Dec; yes; no)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; trans; cong)
-- Removed Reasoning imports as they are missing in stdlib.
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_; zРЅцn; sРЅцs; _РЅЪ_; _РЅц_; _Ріћ_)
open import Data.Empty            using (РіЦ-elim)

open import Ultrametric
open import Contraction

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Discrete ultrametric on Nat: d x y = 0 if x=y else 1
------------------------------------------------------------------------

dNat : Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Nat
dNat x y with x РЅЪ y
... | yes _ = 0
... | no  _ = 1

dNat-refl0 : Рѕђ t Рєњ dNat t t РЅА 0
dNat-refl0 t with t РЅЪ t
... | yes _ = refl
... | no  n = РіЦ-elim (n refl)

id-zeroNat : Рѕђ x Рєњ dNat x x РЅА 0
id-zeroNat x with x РЅЪ x
... | yes _ = refl
... | no  n = РіЦ-elim (n refl)

symNat : Рѕђ x y Рєњ dNat x y РЅА dNat y x
symNat x y with x РЅЪ y | y РЅЪ x
... | yes xy | yes yx = refl
... | no  xy | no  yx = refl
... | yes xy | no  yx = РіЦ-elim (yx (sym xy))
... | no  xy | yes yx = РіЦ-elim (xy (sym yx))

-- ultratriangle: d x z РЅц max (d x y) (d y z)
-- for discrete metric this holds by case split
ultraNat : Рѕђ x y z Рєњ dNat x z РЅц (dNat x y Ріћ dNat y z)
ultraNat x y z with x РЅЪ z
... | yes _ = zРЅцn
... | no xРЅбz with x РЅЪ y | y РЅЪ z
...   | yes xy | yes yz = РіЦ-elim (xРЅбz (trans xy yz))
...   | no  _  | yes yz = sРЅцs zРЅцn
...   | yes xy | no  _  = sРЅцs zРЅцn
...   | no  _  | no  _  = sРЅцs zРЅцn

UNat : Ultrametric Nat
UNat = record
  { d             = dNat
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroNat
  ; symmetric     = symNat
  ; ultratriangle = ultraNat
  }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A projection operator: K projects everything to a fixed target t
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Kproj : Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Nat
Kproj t _ = t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distinctness helper
------------------------------------------------------------------------

dNat-xРЅбy=1 : Рѕђ {x y} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ dNat x y РЅА 1
dNat-xРЅбy=1 {x} {y} xРЅбy with x РЅЪ y
... | yes eq = РіЦ-elim (xРЅбy eq)
... | no _ = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Strict contraction on distinct points (ContractiveРЅб style)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  contractiveРЅб-proj : Рѕђ t Рєњ (Рѕђ {x y} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ dNat (Kproj t x) (Kproj t y) < dNat x y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point uniqueness for projection
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fixed : (Nat Рєњ Nat) Рєњ Nat Рєњ Set
Fixed K a = K a РЅА a

uniqueFixedProj :
  Рѕђ t x y Рєњ
  Fixed (Kproj t) x Рєњ
  Fixed (Kproj t) y Рєњ
  x РЅА y
uniqueFixedProj t x y fx fy =
  trans (sym fx) fy
module DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_; _<_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (_РЅб_; ContractiveРЅб)

_Рѕў_ : Рѕђ {A B C : Set} Рєњ (B Рєњ C) Рєњ (A Рєњ B) Рєњ A Рєњ C
(f Рѕў g) x = f (g x)

infixr 9 _Рѕў_
record NonExpansive {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (f : S Рєњ S) : SetРѓЂ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  field
    nonexp : Рѕђ x y Рєњ d (f x) (f y) РЅц d x y

record DistinctPreserving {S : Set} (g : S Рєњ S) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    preservesРЅб : Рѕђ {x y} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ g x РЅб g y

record OrderLaws : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    le-trans   : Рѕђ {a b c : Nat} Рєњ a РЅц b Рєњ b РЅц c Рєњ a РЅц c
    le-<-trans : Рѕђ {a b c : Nat} Рєњ a РЅц b Рєњ b < c Рєњ a < c
    <-le-trans : Рѕђ {a b c : Nat} Рєњ a < b Рєњ b РЅц c Рєњ a < c

-- If f and g are nonexpansive and h is strictly contractive, then f Рѕў h Рѕў g is strictly contractive.
composeStrict :
  Рѕђ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
    (f g h : S Рєњ S) Рєњ
  OrderLaws Рєњ
  NonExpansive U f Рєњ
  NonExpansive U g Рєњ
  DistinctPreserving g Рєњ
  Contraction.ContractiveРЅб U h Рєњ
  Contraction.ContractiveРЅб U (f Рѕў (h Рѕў g))
composeStrict U f g h laws neF neG dpG sh =
  record
    { contractionРЅб = ╬╗ {x} {y} xРЅбy Рєњ
        let open UMetric.Ultrametric U
            open Contraction.ContractiveРЅб sh
            open OrderLaws laws
            step1 = NonExpansive.nonexp neF (h (g x)) (h (g y))
            step2 = contractionРЅб {x = g x} {y = g y} (DistinctPreserving.preservesРЅб dpG xРЅбy)
            step3 = NonExpansive.nonexp neG x y
        in
        <-le-trans (le-<-trans step1 step2) step3
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (Ріц; tt)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric

record Group (G : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    _РѕЎ_  : G Рєњ G Рєњ G
    e    : G
    inv  : G Рєњ G
    assoc : Рѕђ a b c Рєњ (a РѕЎ b) РѕЎ c РЅА a РѕЎ (b РѕЎ c)
    idL   : Рѕђ a Рєњ e РѕЎ a РЅА a
    invL  : Рѕђ a Рєњ (inv a) РѕЎ a РЅА e

record Isotropy
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (T : S Рєњ S)
       : SetРѓЂ where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  field
    G      : Set
    group  : Group G
    act    : G Рєњ S Рєњ S
    preservesMetric :
      Рѕђ g x y Рєњ d (act g x) (act g y) РЅА d x y
    commutesWithT :
      Рѕђ g x Рєњ T (act g x) РЅА act g (T x)

-- Trivial isotropy: one element group acting by identity.
trivialIsotropy :
  Рѕђ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S Рєњ S) Рєњ
  Isotropy U T
trivialIsotropy U T =
  record
    { G = Ріц
    ; group = record
        { _РѕЎ_ = ╬╗ _ _ Рєњ tt
        ; e = tt
        ; inv = ╬╗ _ Рєњ tt
        ; assoc = ╬╗ _ _ _ Рєњ refl
        ; idL = ╬╗ _ Рєњ refl
        ; invL = ╬╗ _ Рєњ refl
        }
    ; act = ╬╗ _ x Рєњ x
    ; preservesMetric = ╬╗ _ _ _ Рєњ refl
    ; commutesWithT = ╬╗ _ _ Рєњ refl
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.COL where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes
open import DASHI.Core.LensKernel

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ContractionРђЊObstructionРђЊLift (COL)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record COL (S : Nat -> Set) : Set1 where
  field
    E    : forall n -> S n -> Nat
    K    : forall n -> S n -> S n
    Obs  : forall n -> S n -> Bool
    lift : forall n -> S n -> S (suc n)

    -- Contraction inside level n: energy does not increase.
    contract : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> E n (K n x) РЅц E n x

    -- Obstruction is stable under K: if you are obstructed, stepping doesn't РђюsolveРђЮ it magically.
    obs-stable : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> Obs n x РЅА true -> Obs n (K n x) РЅА true

    -- Lift is witness-respecting: the old state is embedded, not destroyed.
    embed-ok : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> Ріц

open COL public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Derived theorem hooks (the Рђюschema theoremsРђЮ)

-- If not obstructed, repeated contraction gives monotone energy sequence.
iterate : forall {A : Set} -> (A -> A) -> Nat -> A -> A
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc k) x = iterate f k (f x)

E-monotone-iter :
  forall {S : Nat -> Set} (C : COL S) ->
  (n : Nat) (k : Nat) (x : S n) ->
  COL.E C n (iterate (COL.K C n) k x) РЅц COL.E C n x
E-monotone-iter C n zero    x = РЅц-refl
E-monotone-iter C n (suc k) x =
  РЅц-trans
    (E-monotone-iter C n k (COL.K C n x))
    (COL.contract C n x)
module DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropyInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_; _xor_)
open import Data.Bool.Properties as BoolP

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym)

-- Two-element group acting by invVec.
boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _РѕЎ_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = ╬╗ a Рєњ a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identity╦А
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

act : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Bool Рєњ RTC.Carrier n Рєњ RTC.Carrier n
act {n} b x = if b then RTC.invVec x else x

preservesMetric :
  Рѕђ {n} Рєњ (g : Bool) Рєњ (x y : RTC.Carrier n) Рєњ
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (act g x) (act g y)
    РЅА UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y
preservesMetric {n} false x y = refl
preservesMetric {n} true x y = FAM.dNatFine-inv x y

commutesWithT :
  Рѕђ {n} Рєњ (g : Bool) Рєњ (x : RTC.Carrier n) Рєњ
  RO.CрхБ (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ (act g x))) РЅА act g (RO.CрхБ (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ x)))
commutesWithT {n} false x = refl
commutesWithT {n} true x = sym (RO.invVec-PрхБ x)

realIsotropyInstance :
  Рѕђ {n} Рєњ
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (╬╗ x Рєњ RO.CрхБ (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ x)))
realIsotropyInstance {n} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionContractionOrthogonalityTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Data.Product public using (_├Ќ_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Minimal algebra: additive group structure (abstract)
-- (You can replace these postulates with your concrete state carrier.)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  S   : Set
  _S+_ : S Рєњ S Рєњ S
  _S-_ : S Рєњ S Рєњ S
  0#  : S

infixl 6 _S+_ _S-_

postulate
  -- Group-ish laws youРђЎll need for Рђюdetail = x - P xРђЮ reasoning
  +-assoc : Рѕђ x y z Рєњ (x S+ y) S+ z РЅА x S+ (y S+ z)
  +-id╩│   : Рѕђ x Рєњ x S+ 0# РЅА x
  +-id╦А   : Рѕђ x Рєњ 0# S+ x РЅА x
  +-inv╩│  : Рѕђ x Рєњ x S- x РЅА 0#

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Metric / norm interface (keep abstract; later bind to your induced norm)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  dist : S Рєњ S Рєњ Set  -- you may replace with РёЮ or Рёџ; kept abstract here

-- A РђюnormРђЮ is distance to 0. (You can swap this for your actual norm.)
postulate
  РѕЦ_РѕЦ : S Рєњ Set
  РѕЦxРѕЦ-def : Рѕђ x Рєњ РѕЦ x РѕЦ РЅА dist x 0#

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Recognisable lift decomposition (your Рђюtelescoping identityРђЮ)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record RecognisableLift (P : S Рєњ S) : Set where
  field
    -- every x decomposes uniquely into coarse + detail:
    coarse   : S Рєњ S
    detail   : S Рєњ S
    split    : Рѕђ x Рєњ x РЅА coarse x S+ detail x

    -- recognisable uniqueness: if x = c+d = c'+d' with both c,c' fixed by P
    -- and both d,d' in the fiber kernel, then equal (abstracted)
    uniq :
      Рѕђ x c d c' d' Рєњ
      x РЅА c S+ d Рєњ
      x РЅА c' S+ d' Рєњ
      P c РЅА c Рєњ
      P c' РЅА c' Рєњ
      P d РЅА 0# Рєњ
      P d' РЅА 0# Рєњ
      (c РЅА c') ├Ќ (d РЅА d')

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Non-expansive idempotent projection axioms
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record NonExpansiveProjection (P : S Рєњ S) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    idem  : Рѕђ x Рєњ P (P x) РЅА P x
    nonexp : Рѕђ x y Рєњ dist (P x) (P y) РЅА dist x y
    -- (If you want РЅц instead of РЅА, change dist codomain to Рёџ/РёЮ and use РЅц.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Orthogonality: Рђюno double countingРђЮ in the induced quadratic energy
--
-- This is the *test* you want Agda to force:
--   from RecognisableLift + NonExpansiveProjection (+ stability axiom),
--   derive Pythagorean split for a quadratic norm and orthogonality.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record OrthogonalSplit (P : S Рєњ S) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    РЪѓ-pred : S Рєњ S Рєњ Set          -- РђюorthogonalРђЮ predicate (abstract)
    pythag :
      Рѕђ x Рєњ
      let c = P x
          d = x S- P x
      in  РѕЦ x РѕЦ РЅА (РѕЦ c РѕЦ) ├Ќ (РѕЦ d РѕЦ)   -- placeholder shape; replace with numeric identity
    orth :
      Рѕђ x Рєњ
      let c = P x
          d = x S- P x
      in  РЪѓ-pred c d

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The Master Theorem (as a test harness)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  -- Stability premise: the multiscale hierarchy must forbid leakage.
  -- You can replace this with your contractive fixed-point stability lemma.
  StabilityNoLeakage :
    (P : S Рєњ S) Рєњ Set

postulate
  MasterTheorem :
    (P : S Рєњ S) Рєњ
    RecognisableLift P Рєњ
    NonExpansiveProjection P Рєњ
    StabilityNoLeakage P Рєњ
    OrthogonalSplit P

-- Fixed locality radius (nontrivial, but simple).
radius : Nat

local : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ Set
local {n} x y = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y РЅц radius

preservesLocality :
  Рѕђ {n} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  local x y Рєњ
  local (RO.CрхБ (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ x))) (RO.CрхБ (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ y)))
preservesLocality {n} x y h =
  let
    open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n})
    step1 : d (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ x)) (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ y)) РЅц d (RO.RрхБ x) (RO.RрхБ y)
    step1 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpPрхБ {n}) (RO.RрхБ x) (RO.RрхБ y)
    step2 : d (RO.RрхБ x) (RO.RрхБ y) РЅц d x y
    step2 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpRрхБ {n}) x y
    step3 : d (RO.CрхБ (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ x))) (RO.CрхБ (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ y)))
            РЅц d (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ x)) (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ y))
    step3 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpCрхБ {n}) (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ x)) (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ y))
  in
  NatP.РЅц-trans (NatP.РЅц-trans step3 step1) (NatP.РЅц-trans step2 h)

  Рѕђ {n} Рєњ
  RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (╬╗ x Рєњ RO.CрхБ (RO.PрхБ (RO.RрхБ x)))

    ; preservesLocality = preservesLocality {n}

_РЅб_ : {A : Set} Рєњ A Рєњ A Рєњ Set

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.NoGlobalAttractor where

-- Iteration

iterate f zero    x = x

-- РђюEventually constantРђЮ orbit at a.

EventuallyConst f x a = ╬Б Nat (╬╗ N Рєњ Рѕђ n Рєњ iterate f (N + n) x РЅА a)

-- Global attractor = same a for all x.
GlobalAttractor : Рѕђ {S : Set} Рєњ (S Рєњ S) Рєњ Set
GlobalAttractor f = ╬Б _ (╬╗ a Рєњ Рѕђ x Рєњ EventuallyConst f x a)

-- (In a finite/discrete world, invertible dynamics canРђЎt collapse all orbits to one point unless singleton.)

  invertible-nontrivial-no-attractor :
    Рѕђ {S : Set} {U : S Рєњ S} Рєњ
    Invertible U Рєњ
    (╬Б S (╬╗ x Рєњ ╬Б S (╬╗ y Рєњ ┬г (x РЅА y)))) Рєњ
    ┬г GlobalAttractor U

  field

  (ker : SpinData.Spin D Рєњ Set)

  SpinDoubleCover D
spinDoubleCover-witness D ker kerРіє┬▒1 surj =
  record { hom = SpinData.toSO D ; kernel = ker ; kernelРіє┬▒1 = kerРіє┬▒1 ; surjective = surj }

      Рѕђ i Рєњ (H bracket Hрхб i) РЅА H

    -- [H, H] = Hрхб(...)

      ╬Б Idx (╬╗ k Рєњ (H bracket H) РЅА Hрхб k)

module DASHI.Algebra.UnitaryVsCollapse where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Nullary      using (┬г_)
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_)
open import Data.Empty            using (РіЦ; РіЦ-elim)

-- A minimal invertible step system with a Nat-valued measure.
record InvertibleNat (S : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    step  : S Рєњ S
    inv   : S Рєњ S
    left  : Рѕђ s Рєњ inv (step s) РЅА s
    right : Рѕђ s Рєњ step (inv s) РЅА s
    H     : S Рєњ Nat

open InvertibleNat public

-- Iteration
iterate : Рѕђ {S : Set} Рєњ (S Рєњ S) Рєњ Nat Рєњ S Рєњ S
iterate f zero    s = s
iterate f (suc n) s = iterate f n (f s)

-- If you have strict decrease everywhere, you get an infinite descent
-- along iterates, which is impossible in Nat.
--
-- To keep this module lightweight, we package the Рђюno infinite descentРђЮ
-- fact as a single lemma that can be discharged from stdlib later.
--
-- (If you want, I can give the fully discharged stdlib proof too.)
postulate
  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    Рѕђ {S : Set} (H : S Рєњ Nat) (f : S Рєњ S) (sРѓђ : S) Рєњ
    (Рѕђ s Рєњ H (f s) < H s) Рєњ РіЦ

-- Main theorem: in an inhabited system, Рђюstrict collapse everywhereРђЮ is impossible.
no-global-strict-collapse :
  Рѕђ {S : Set} (U : InvertibleNat S) Рєњ
  (sРѓђ : S) Рєњ
  ┬г (Рѕђ s Рєњ H U (step U s) < H U s)
no-global-strict-collapse U sРѓђ strict =
  NatNoInfiniteDescent (H U) (step U) sРѓђ strict

module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterUltrametric15 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym)
open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_; _<_; _Ріћ_; _РѕИ_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (РЅц-refl; РЅц-trans; mРЅцmРіћn; mРЅцnРіћm)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_)
-- Removed Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Base.Raw as it's not needed here.
-- Removed Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Nat as it's not needed here.

open import Ultrametric
open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 using (Mask15)

lcpLen : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Bool n Рєњ Vec Bool n Рєњ Nat
lcpLen [] [] = 0
lcpLen (true  Рѕи xs) (true  Рѕи ys) = suc (lcpLen xs ys)
lcpLen (false Рѕи xs) (false Рѕи ys) = suc (lcpLen xs ys)
lcpLen (_ Рѕи _) (_ Рѕи _) = 0

len : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Bool n Рєњ Nat
len []       = 0
len (_ Рѕи xs) = suc (len xs)

dMask : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Bool n Рєњ Vec Bool n Рєњ Nat
dMask {n} x y = len {n} x РѕИ lcpLen x y

-- id-zero
lcpLen-self-eq : Рѕђ {n} (m : Vec Bool n) Рєњ lcpLen m m РЅА len {n} m
lcpLen-self-eq [] = refl
lcpLen-self-eq (true  Рѕи xs) = cong suc (lcpLen-self-eq xs)
lcpLen-self-eq (false Рѕи xs) = cong suc (lcpLen-self-eq xs)

postulate
  id-zeroMask : Рѕђ m Рєњ dMask {15} m m РЅА 0

-- symmetric
lcpLen-symmetric : Рѕђ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) Рєњ lcpLen x y РЅА lcpLen y x
lcpLen-symmetric [] [] = refl
lcpLen-symmetric (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys) with x | y
... | true | true = cong suc (lcpLen-symmetric xs ys)
... | false | false = cong suc (lcpLen-symmetric xs ys)
... | true | false = refl
... | false | true = refl

postulate
  dMask-symmetric : Рѕђ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) Рєњ dMask {n} x y РЅА dMask {n} y x

symMask : Рѕђ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) Рєњ dMask {n} x y РЅА dMask {n} y x
symMask = dMask-symmetric

-- ultratriangle
postulate
  lcpLen-ultratriangle :
    Рѕђ {n} (x y z : Vec Bool n) Рєњ
    lcpLen x y Ріћ lcpLen y z РЅц lcpLen x z

postulate
  ultraMask : Рѕђ x y z Рєњ dMask {15} x z РЅц (dMask {15} x y Ріћ dMask {15} y z)

UMask15 : Ultrametric Mask15
UMask15 = record
  { d             = dMask {15}
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroMask
  ; symmetric     = symMask {15}
  ; ultratriangle = ultraMask
  }module DASHI.Algebra.CCR where

open import Agda.Primitive
open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

-- An abstract carrier for operators. This needs to be parameterized by a level.
-- We use Level0 for now, but this could be (РёЊ : Level) : Set (lsuc РёЊ) as suggested.
record Op (S : Set) (РёЊ : Level) : Set (lsuc РёЊ) where
  field
    apply : S Рєњ S

-- A basic definition of composition (operator product)
_Рѕў_ : Рѕђ {РёЊРѓЂ РёЊРѓѓ РёЊРѓЃ} {A : Set РёЊРѓЂ} {B : Set РёЊРѓѓ} {C : Set РёЊРѓЃ} Рєњ (B Рєњ C) Рєњ (A Рєњ B) Рєњ (A Рєњ C)
f Рѕў g = ╬╗ x Рєњ f (g x)

_OpРѕў_ : Рѕђ {S РёЊ} Рєњ Op S РёЊ Рєњ Op S РёЊ Рєњ Op S РёЊ
_OpРѕў_ {S} {РёЊ} op1 op2 = record { apply = (Op.apply op1) Рѕў (Op.apply op2) }

-- Commutator for two operators

module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 where

FactorCount = 15

Mask15 : Set
Mask15 = Vec Bool FactorCount

fullMask : Mask15

emptyMask : Mask15
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

-- Pointwise AND (same length, total)
boolAnd : Bool Рєњ Bool Рєњ Bool
boolAnd true true = true
boolAnd _    _    = false

_РѕД_ : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Bool n Рєњ Vec Bool n Рєњ Vec Bool n
_РѕД_ {zero} [] [] = []

module DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat as Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Contraction using (_РЅб_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym; subst)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_; _РЅц_; _РЅЦ_; _РѕИ_; zРЅцn; sРЅцs)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Product using (_,_)

open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse; _Рѕи╩│_; cast; init; last; initLast)

congРѓѓ : Рѕђ {A B C : Set} {xРѓЂ xРѓѓ : A} {yРѓЂ yРѓѓ : B}
        (g : A Рєњ B Рєњ C) Рєњ
        xРѓЂ РЅА xРѓѓ Рєњ yРѓЂ РЅА yРѓѓ Рєњ g xРѓЂ yРѓЂ РЅА g xРѓѓ yРѓѓ
congРѓѓ g refl refl = refl

-- Fine agreement metric: use agreement depth on reversed vectors (suffix agreement).
agreeDepthFine : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Nat
agreeDepthFine x y = AM.agreeDepth (reverse x) (reverse y)

dNatFine : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Nat
dNatFine x y = AM.dNat (reverse x) (reverse y)

dNatFine-inv :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  dNatFine (map inv x) (map inv y) РЅА dNatFine x y
dNatFine-inv x y =
  let
    rx = reverse x
    ry = reverse y
    rx-inv : reverse (map inv x) РЅА map inv rx
    rx-inv = sym (map-reverse inv x)
    ry-inv : reverse (map inv y) РЅА map inv ry
    ry-inv = sym (map-reverse inv y)
  in
  trans
    (cong (╬╗ a Рєњ AM.dNat a (reverse (map inv y))) rx-inv)
    (trans
      (cong (╬╗ b Рєњ AM.dNat (map inv rx) b) ry-inv)
      (AM.dNat-inv rx ry)
    )

reverseРЅб : Рѕђ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ reverse x РЅб reverse y
reverseРЅб xРЅбy revРЅА = xРЅбy (reverse-injective revРЅА)

dNatFine-zeroРєњeq :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ dNatFine x y РЅА 0 Рєњ x РЅА y
dNatFine-zeroРєњeq x y dРЅА0 =
  reverse-injective (AM.dNat-zeroРєњeq (reverse x) (reverse y) dРЅА0)

dNatFine-positive :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ 0 < dNatFine x y
dNatFine-positive xРЅбy = AM.dNat-positive (reverseРЅб xРЅбy)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Agreement-depth monotonicity under pointwise maps

agreeDepth-mapРЅц :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (f : Trit Рєњ Trit) (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  AM.agreeDepth x y РЅц AM.agreeDepth (map f x) (map f y)
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {n = Nat.zero} f [] [] = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (neg Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) with f neg
... | neg = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
... | zer = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
... | pos = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (zer Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) with f zer
... | neg = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
... | zer = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
... | pos = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (pos Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) with f pos
... | neg = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
... | zer = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
... | pos = sРЅцs (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f xs ys)
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (neg Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (neg Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (zer Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (zer Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (pos Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-mapРЅц {suc n} f (pos Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn

dNatFine-mapРЅц :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (f : Trit Рєњ Trit) (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  dNatFine (map f x) (map f y) РЅц dNatFine x y
dNatFine-mapРЅц {n} f x y =
  let
    rx-map : reverse (map f x) РЅА map f (reverse x)
    rx-map = sym (map-reverse f x)
    ry-map : reverse (map f y) РЅА map f (reverse y)
    ry-map = sym (map-reverse f y)
    step : AM.dNat (map f (reverse x)) (map f (reverse y)) РЅц AM.dNat (reverse x) (reverse y)
    step = NatP.РѕИ-mono╩│-РЅц n (agreeDepth-mapРЅц f (reverse x) (reverse y))
  in
  NatP.РЅц-trans
    (NatP.РЅц-reflexive (congРѓѓ AM.dNat rx-map ry-map))
    step

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Agreement depth for append (prefix metric on reverse)

agreeDepth-++РЅЦ :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (a b : Vec Trit m) (c : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  AM.agreeDepth (a ++ c) (b ++ c) РЅЦ AM.agreeDepth a b
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] c = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) c =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++РЅЦ as bs c)
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) c =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++РЅЦ as bs c)
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) c =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++РЅЦ as bs c)
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) c = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) c = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) c = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) c = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) c = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++РЅЦ {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) c = zРЅцn

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Reverse of snoc: reverse (xs Рѕи╩│ a) = a Рѕи reverse xs

reverse-Рѕи╩│ : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit n) (a : Trit) Рєњ
  reverse (xs Рѕи╩│ a) РЅА a Рѕи reverse xs
reverse-Рѕи╩│ [] a = reverse-Рѕи a []
reverse-Рѕи╩│ (x Рѕи xs) a
  rewrite reverse-Рѕи x (xs Рѕи╩│ a)
        | reverse-Рѕи╩│ xs a
        | reverse-Рѕи x xs
  = refl

agreeDepth-cast :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (eq : m РЅА n) (x y : Vec Trit m) Рєњ
  AM.agreeDepth (cast eq x) (cast eq y) РЅА AM.agreeDepth x y
agreeDepth-cast refl x y
  rewrite cast-is-id refl x
        | cast-is-id refl y
  = refl

dNat-cast :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (eq : m РЅА n) (x y : Vec Trit m) Рєњ
  AM.dNat (cast eq x) (cast eq y) РЅА AM.dNat x y
dNat-cast refl x y
  rewrite cast-is-id refl x
        | cast-is-id refl y
  = refl

-- ShiftTail monotonicity on fine agreement

agreeDepth-++-mono :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (u v u' v' : Vec Trit m) (p q : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  AM.agreeDepth u v РЅц AM.agreeDepth u' v' Рєњ
  AM.agreeDepth (u ++ p) (v ++ q) РЅц AM.agreeDepth (u' ++ p) (v' ++ q)
agreeDepth-++-mono {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] [] [] p q h = NatP.РЅц-refl
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи us) (neg Рѕи vs) (neg Рѕи us') (neg Рѕи vs') p q (sРЅцs hРЅц) =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hРЅц)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи us) (neg Рѕи vs) (zer Рѕи us') (zer Рѕи vs') p q (sРЅцs hРЅц) =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hРЅц)

agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи us) (zer Рѕи vs) (zer Рѕи us') (zer Рѕи vs') p q (sРЅцs hРЅц) =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hРЅц)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи us) (zer Рѕи vs) (pos Рѕи us') (pos Рѕи vs') p q (sРЅцs hРЅц) =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hРЅц)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи us) (pos Рѕи vs) (neg Рѕи us') (neg Рѕи vs') p q (sРЅцs hРЅц) =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hРЅц)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи us) (pos Рѕи vs) (zer Рѕи us') (zer Рѕи vs') p q (sРЅцs hРЅц) =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hРЅц)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи us) (pos Рѕи vs) (pos Рѕи us') (pos Рѕи vs') p q (sРЅцs hРЅц) =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hРЅц)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи us) (zer Рѕи vs) u' v' p q h = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи us) (pos Рѕи vs) u' v' p q h = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи us) (neg Рѕи vs) u' v' p q h = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи us) (pos Рѕи vs) u' v' p q h = zРЅцn

agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи us) (zer Рѕи vs) u' v' p q h = zРЅцn

agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (u v : Vec Trit m) (p q : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit Рєњ Trit) Рєњ
  AM.agreeDepth (u ++ p) (v ++ q) РЅц AM.agreeDepth (u ++ map f p) (v ++ map f q)
agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] p q f = agreeDepth-mapРЅц f p q
agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи us) (neg Рѕи vs) p q f =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи us) (zer Рѕи vs) p q f =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи us) (pos Рѕи vs) p q f =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи us) (zer Рѕи vs) p q f = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {suc m} {n} (neg Рѕи us) (pos Рѕи vs) p q f = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {suc m} {n} (zer Рѕи us) (neg Рѕи vs) p q f = zРЅцn
