agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи us) (neg Рѕи vs) p q f = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц {suc m} {n} (pos Рѕи us) (zer Рѕи vs) p q f = zРЅцn

agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (a b : Vec Trit n) (x y : Trit) Рєњ
  AM.agreeDepth (a Рѕи╩│ x) (b Рѕи╩│ y) РЅц suc (AM.agreeDepth a b)
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg neg = sРЅцs zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer zer = sРЅцs zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos pos = sРЅцs zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg zer = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg pos = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer neg = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer pos = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos neg = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos zer = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (neg Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) x y =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц as bs x y)
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (zer Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) x y =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц as bs x y)
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (pos Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) x y =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц as bs x y)
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (neg Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) x y = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (neg Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) x y = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (zer Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) x y = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (zer Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) x y = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (pos Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) x y = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц {suc n} (pos Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) x y = zРЅцn

agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (a b : Trit) (as bs : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  AM.agreeDepth (a Рѕи as) (b Рѕи bs) РЅц suc (AM.agreeDepth as bs)
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц neg neg as bs = sРЅцs NatP.РЅц-refl
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц zer zer as bs = sРЅцs NatP.РЅц-refl
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц pos pos as bs = sРЅцs NatP.РЅц-refl
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц neg zer as bs = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц neg pos as bs = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц zer neg as bs = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц zer pos as bs = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц pos neg as bs = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц pos zer as bs = zРЅцn

agreeDepthFine-shiftTailРЅЦ :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  agreeDepthFine t1 t2 РЅц agreeDepthFine (TCP.shiftTail t1) (TCP.shiftTail t2)
agreeDepthFine-shiftTailРЅЦ {k = Nat.zero} [] [] = zРЅцn
agreeDepthFine-shiftTailРЅЦ {suc k} (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys) =
  NatP.РЅц-trans
    (subst
      (╬╗ v Рєњ v РЅц suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs) (reverse ys)))
      (sym lhs1)
      (agreeDepth-Рѕи╩│РЅц (reverse xs) (reverse ys) x y))
    (NatP.РЅц-reflexive (sym lhs))
  where
    lhs1 : agreeDepthFine (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys)
           РЅА AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs Рѕи╩│ x) (reverse ys Рѕи╩│ y)
    lhs1 rewrite reverse-Рѕи x xs | reverse-Рѕи y ys = refl
    lhs : AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.shiftTail (x Рѕи xs)))
                        (reverse (TCP.shiftTail (y Рѕи ys)))
          РЅА suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs) (reverse ys))
    lhs rewrite reverse-Рѕи╩│ xs zer | reverse-Рѕи╩│ ys zer = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive for shiftTail (tail-only)

dNatFine-shiftTailРЅц :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  dNatFine (TCP.shiftTail t1) (TCP.shiftTail t2) РЅц dNatFine t1 t2
dNatFine-shiftTailРЅц {k} t1 t2 =
  NatP.РѕИ-mono╩│-РЅц k (agreeDepthFine-shiftTailРЅЦ t1 t2)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive for projTail (tail-only)

agreeDepthFine-projTailРЅЦ :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  agreeDepthFine t1 t2 РЅц agreeDepthFine (TCP.projTail t1) (TCP.projTail t2)
agreeDepthFine-projTailРЅЦ {k = Nat.zero} [] [] = zРЅцn
agreeDepthFine-projTailРЅЦ {k = Nat.suc k} (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys) =
  NatP.РЅц-trans bound (NatP.РЅц-reflexive (sym (trans r1 r2)))
  where
    init-Рѕи╩│-last : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc n)) Рєњ init t Рѕи╩│ last t РЅА t
    init-Рѕи╩│-last t with initLast t
    ... | ys , y , eq = sym eq

    reverse-init-last :
      Рѕђ {n : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc n)) Рєњ
      reverse t РЅА last t Рѕи reverse (init t)
    reverse-init-last t =
      trans
        (cong reverse (sym (init-Рѕи╩│-last t)))
        (reverse-Рѕи╩│ (init t) (last t))

    r1 : agreeDepthFine (TCP.projTail (x Рѕи xs)) (TCP.projTail (y Рѕи ys))
         РЅА AM.agreeDepth (zer Рѕи reverse (init (x Рѕи xs))) (zer Рѕи reverse (init (y Рѕи ys)))
    r1 rewrite reverse-Рѕи╩│ (init (x Рѕи xs)) zer | reverse-Рѕи╩│ (init (y Рѕи ys)) zer = refl

    r2 : AM.agreeDepth (zer Рѕи reverse (init (x Рѕи xs))) (zer Рѕи reverse (init (y Рѕи ys)))
         РЅА suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x Рѕи xs))) (reverse (init (y Рѕи ys))))
    r2 = refl
    lhs1 : agreeDepthFine (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys)
           РЅА AM.agreeDepth (last (x Рѕи xs) Рѕи reverse (init (x Рѕи xs)))
                           (last (y Рѕи ys) Рѕи reverse (init (y Рѕи ys)))
    lhs1 rewrite reverse-init-last (x Рѕи xs)
                | reverse-init-last (y Рѕи ys)
      = refl
    bound :
      agreeDepthFine (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys)
      РЅц suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x Рѕи xs))) (reverse (init (y Рѕи ys))))
    bound =
      subst
        (╬╗ v Рєњ v РЅц suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x Рѕи xs))) (reverse (init (y Рѕи ys)))))
        (sym lhs1)
        (agreeDepth-РѕиРЅц (last (x Рѕи xs)) (last (y Рѕи ys))
                       (reverse (init (x Рѕи xs))) (reverse (init (y Рѕи ys))))

dNatFine-projTailРЅц :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  dNatFine (TCP.projTail t1) (TCP.projTail t2) РЅц dNatFine t1 t2
dNatFine-projTailРЅц {k} t1 t2 =
  NatP.РѕИ-mono╩│-РЅц k (agreeDepthFine-projTailРЅЦ t1 t2)

dNatFine-++ :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') РЅА
  AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
dNatFine-++ {m} {n} c c' t t' =
  let
    eq : m + n РЅА n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx : reverse (c ++ t) РЅА cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse c)
    rx = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c t))
    ry : reverse (c' ++ t') РЅА cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    ry = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c' t'))
  in
  trans
    (congРѓѓ AM.dNat rx ry)
    (dNat-cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c'))

dNatFine-++-mapРЅц :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit Рєњ Trit) Рєњ
  dNatFine (map f c ++ t) (map f c' ++ t') РЅц dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-mapРЅц {m} {n} c c' t t' f =
  let
    eq : m + n РЅА n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx-cast : reverse (map f c ++ t) РЅА cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse (map f c))
    rx-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq (map f c) t))
    ry-cast : reverse (map f c' ++ t') РЅА cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ reverse (map f c'))
    ry-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq (map f c') t'))
    rx-map : reverse (map f c ++ t) РЅА cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ map f (reverse c))
    rx-map = trans rx-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (reverse t ++_) (sym (map-reverse f c))))
    ry-map : reverse (map f c' ++ t') РЅА cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ map f (reverse c'))
    ry-map = trans ry-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (reverse t' ++_) (sym (map-reverse f c'))))
    step : AM.dNat (reverse t ++ map f (reverse c))
                   (reverse t' ++ map f (reverse c'))
           РЅц AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c)
                    (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    step = NatP.РѕИ-mono╩│-РЅц (n + m)
             (agreeDepth-++-mapРЅц (reverse t) (reverse t') (reverse c) (reverse c') f)

    rhs : dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') РЅА
          AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    rhs = dNatFine-++ c c' t t'
  in
  NatP.РЅц-trans
    (NatP.РЅц-reflexive (trans (congРѓѓ AM.dNat rx-map ry-map) (dNat-cast (sym eq) _ _)))
    (NatP.РЅц-trans step (NatP.РЅц-reflexive (sym rhs)))

dNatFine-++-shiftTailРЅц :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  dNatFine (c ++ TCP.shiftTail t) (c' ++ TCP.shiftTail t') РЅц dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-shiftTailРЅц {m} {n} c c' t t'
  rewrite dNatFine-++ c c' (TCP.shiftTail t) (TCP.shiftTail t')
        | dNatFine-++ c c' t t' =
  let
    depthРЅц :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      РЅц AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t) ++ reverse c)
                     (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t') ++ reverse c')
    depthРЅц =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t)) (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepthFine-shiftTailРЅЦ t t')
  in
  NatP.РѕИ-mono╩│-РЅц (n + m) depthРЅц

dNatFine-++-projTailРЅц :
  Рѕђ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  dNatFine (c ++ TCP.projTail t) (c' ++ TCP.projTail t') РЅц dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-projTailРЅц {m} {n} c c' t t'
  rewrite dNatFine-++ c c' (TCP.projTail t) (TCP.projTail t')
        | dNatFine-++ c c' t t' =
  let
    depthРЅц :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      РЅц AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.projTail t) ++ reverse c)
                     (reverse (TCP.projTail t') ++ reverse c')
    depthРЅц =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (reverse (TCP.projTail t)) (reverse (TCP.projTail t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepthFine-projTailРЅЦ t t')
  in
  NatP.РѕИ-mono╩│-РЅц (n + m) depthРЅц

ultrametricVec : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit n)
ultrametricVec {n} =
  record
    { d = dNatFine
    ; id-zero = ╬╗ x Рєњ UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x)
    ; symmetric = ╬╗ x y Рєњ UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x) (reverse y)
    ; ultratriangle = ╬╗ x y z Рєњ UMetric.Ultrametric.ultratriangle AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x) (reverse y) (reverse z)
    }
module DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_; _<_; _РЅЦ_; _Ріћ_; _РіЊ_; _РѕИ_; zРЅцn; sРЅцs)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Sum using (injРѓЂ; injРѓѓ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; map)
open import Contraction using (_РЅб_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (inv)

-- Agreement depth (longest common prefix) for Vec Trit n.
agreeDepth : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Nat
agreeDepth [] [] = zero
agreeDepth (neg Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth (zer Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth (pos Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth _ _ = zero

-- Distance: reversed depth.
dNat : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Nat
dNat {n} x y = n РѕИ agreeDepth x y

agreeDepth-self : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x : Vec Trit n) Рєњ agreeDepth x x РЅА n
agreeDepth-self [] = refl
agreeDepth-self (neg Рѕи xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl
agreeDepth-self (zer Рѕи xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl
agreeDepth-self (pos Рѕи xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl

agreeDepth-sym : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ agreeDepth x y РЅА agreeDepth y x
agreeDepth-sym [] [] = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = refl

agreeDepth-inv :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  agreeDepth (map inv x) (map inv y) РЅА agreeDepth x y
agreeDepth-inv [] [] = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = refl

dNat-inv :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  dNat (map inv x) (map inv y) РЅА dNat x y
dNat-inv {n} x y = cong (╬╗ k Рєњ n РѕИ k) (agreeDepth-inv x y)

agreeDepthРЅцn : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ agreeDepth x y РЅц n
agreeDepthРЅцn [] [] = zРЅцn
agreeDepthРЅцn (neg Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = sРЅцs (agreeDepthРЅцn xs ys)
agreeDepthРЅцn (zer Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = sРЅцs (agreeDepthРЅцn xs ys)
agreeDepthРЅцn (pos Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = sРЅцs (agreeDepthРЅцn xs ys)
agreeDepthРЅцn (neg Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepthРЅцn (neg Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepthРЅцn (zer Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepthРЅцn (zer Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepthРЅцn (pos Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn
agreeDepthРЅцn (pos Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) = zРЅцn

agreeDepth-eqРєњeq : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ agreeDepth x y РЅА n Рєњ x РЅА y
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq [] [] _ = refl
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (neg Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) eq =
  cong (neg Рѕи_) (agreeDepth-eqРєњeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (zer Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) eq =
  cong (zer Рѕи_) (agreeDepth-eqРєњeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (pos Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) eq =
  cong (pos Рѕи_) (agreeDepth-eqРєњeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (neg Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (neg Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (zer Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (zer Рѕи xs) (pos Рѕи ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (pos Рѕи xs) (neg Рѕи ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqРєњeq (pos Рѕи xs) (zer Рѕи ys) ()

dNat-zeroРєњeq : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) Рєњ dNat x y РЅА 0 Рєњ x РЅА y
dNat-zeroРєњeq {n} x y dРЅА0 =
  let
    depthРЅЦ : n РЅц agreeDepth x y
    depthРЅЦ = NatP.mРѕИnРЅА0РЄњmРЅцn dРЅА0
    depthРЅц : agreeDepth x y РЅц n
    depthРЅц = agreeDepthРЅцn x y
    depthРЅА : agreeDepth x y РЅА n
    depthРЅА = NatP.РЅц-antisym depthРЅц depthРЅЦ
  in
  agreeDepth-eqРєњeq x y depthРЅА

dNat-nonzero : Рѕђ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ dNat x y РЅб 0
dNat-nonzero xРЅбy dРЅА0 = xРЅбy (dNat-zeroРєњeq _ _ dРЅА0)

dNat-positive : Рѕђ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ 0 < dNat x y
dNat-positive xРЅбy = NatP.nРЅб0РЄњn>0 (dNat-nonzero xРЅбy)

-- Strong triangle inequality for agreement depth (prefix metric).
agreeDepth-triangle :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y z : Vec Trit n) Рєњ
  (agreeDepth x y РіЊ agreeDepth y z) РЅц agreeDepth x z
agreeDepth-triangle [] [] [] = zРЅцn
agreeDepth-triangle (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys) (z Рѕи zs) with x | y | z
... | neg | neg | neg =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | zer | zer | zer =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | pos | pos | pos =
  sРЅцs (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | neg | neg | zer = zРЅцn
... | neg | neg | pos = zРЅцn
... | zer | zer | neg = zРЅцn
... | zer | zer | pos = zРЅцn
... | pos | pos | neg = zРЅцn
... | pos | pos | zer = zРЅцn
... | neg | zer | _ = zРЅцn
... | neg | pos | _ = zРЅцn
... | zer | neg | _ = zРЅцn
... | zer | pos | _ = zРЅцn
... | pos | neg | _ = zРЅцn
... | pos | zer | _ = zРЅцn

-- Ultrametric inequality: d x z РЅц max (d x y) (d y z)
ultraNat : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y z : Vec Trit n) Рєњ dNat x z РЅц (dNat x y Ріћ dNat y z)
ultraNat {n} x y z with NatP.РЅц-total (agreeDepth x y) (agreeDepth y z)
... | injРѓЂ xyРЅцyz =
  let
    minРЅА : (agreeDepth x y РіЊ agreeDepth y z) РЅА agreeDepth x y
    minРЅА = NatP.mРЅцnРЄњmРіЊnРЅАm xyРЅцyz
    depthРЅц : agreeDepth x y РЅц agreeDepth x z
    depthРЅц = NatP.РЅц-trans (NatP.РЅц-reflexive (sym minРЅА)) (agreeDepth-triangle x y z)
    depthРЅЦ : agreeDepth x z РЅЦ agreeDepth x y
    depthРЅЦ = depthРЅц
    step1 : dNat x z РЅц dNat x y
    step1 = NatP.РѕИ-mono (NatP.РЅц-refl {n}) depthРЅЦ
    step2 : dNat x z РЅц (dNat x y Ріћ dNat y z)
    step2 = NatP.РЅц-trans step1 (NatP.mРЅцmРіћn (dNat x y) (dNat y z))
  in step2
... | injРѓѓ yzРЅцxy =
  let
    minРЅА : (agreeDepth x y РіЊ agreeDepth y z) РЅА agreeDepth y z
    minРЅА = NatP.mРЅЦnРЄњmРіЊnРЅАn yzРЅцxy
    depthРЅц : agreeDepth y z РЅц agreeDepth x z
    depthРЅц = NatP.РЅц-trans (NatP.РЅц-reflexive (sym minРЅА)) (agreeDepth-triangle x y z)
    depthРЅЦ : agreeDepth x z РЅЦ agreeDepth y z
    depthРЅЦ = depthРЅц
    step1 : dNat x z РЅц dNat y z
    step1 = NatP.РѕИ-mono (NatP.РЅц-refl {n}) depthРЅЦ
    step2 : dNat x z РЅц (dNat x y Ріћ dNat y z)
    step2 = NatP.РЅц-trans step1 (NatP.mРЅцnРіћm (dNat x y) (dNat y z))
  in step2

ultrametricVec : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit n)
ultrametricVec {n} =
  record
    { d = dNat
    ; id-zero = ╬╗ x Рєњ
        trans
          (cong (╬╗ k Рєњ n РѕИ k) (agreeDepth-self x))
          (NatP.nРѕИnРЅА0 n)
    ; symmetric = ╬╗ x y Рєњ
        cong (╬╗ k Рєњ n РѕИ k) (agreeDepth-sym x y)
    ; ultratriangle = ultraNat
    }

module DASHI.Combinatorics.FractranCOL where

open import Data.Nat renaming (РёЋ to Nat)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatProp using
  (РЅц-refl; РЅц-trans; <-trans; +-mono-РЅц; <-step)
open import Data.Maybe using (Maybe; just; nothing)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_РЅА_; refl; cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- State: exponent vector for primes [2,3,5,7,11] (5 lanes)
-- lane 0=2, 1=3, 2=5, 3=7, 4=11

EV5 : Set
EV5 = Vec Nat 5

get : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Nat n Рєњ Nat Рєњ Nat
get (x Рѕи xs) zero    = x
get (x Рѕи xs) (suc i) = get xs i
get []       _       = zero

set : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Nat n Рєњ Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Vec Nat n
set (x Рѕи xs) zero    v = v Рѕи xs
set (x Рѕи xs) (suc i) v = x Рѕи set xs i v
set []       _       _ = []

dec1 : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Nat n Рєњ Nat Рєњ Maybe (Vec Nat n)
dec1 {n} ev i with get ev i
... | zero  = nothing
... | suc m = just (set ev i m)

inc1 : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Nat n Рєњ Nat Рєњ Vec Nat n
inc1 ev i = set ev i (suc (get ev i))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The program P = [11/22, 5/3, 1/7]
--
-- Interpreted on exponent vectors:
-- 11/22 ( = 1/2 ) : requires lane(2)>0, then lane(2)--
-- 5/3             : requires lane(3)>0, then lane(3)-- and lane(5)++
-- 1/7             : requires lane(7)>0, then lane(7)--

data Rule : Set where
  r1122 r53 r17 : Rule

apply : Rule Рєњ EV5 Рєњ Maybe EV5
apply r1122 ev = dec1 ev 0
apply r53   ev with dec1 ev 1
... | nothing = nothing
... | just e  = just (inc1 e 2)
apply r17   ev = dec1 ev 3

-- First-applicable (deterministic) scan order:
step : EV5 Рєњ Maybe EV5
step ev with apply r1122 ev
... | just ev' = just ev'
... | nothing with apply r53 ev
...   | just ev' = just ev'
...   | nothing  = apply r17 ev

Obs : EV5 Рєњ Set
Obs ev = step ev РЅА nothing

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Rank / energy: a + b + d where lanes are 2,3,7 (0,1,3)
E : EV5 Рєњ Nat
E ev = get ev 0 + get ev 1 + get ev 3

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lemmas: each successful rule application decreases E by 1

postulate
  E-dec2 : Рѕђ {ev ev'} Рєњ apply r1122 ev РЅА just ev' Рєњ E ev' < E ev
  E-dec3 : Рѕђ {ev ev'} Рєњ apply r53 ev РЅА just ev' Рєњ E ev' < E ev
  E-dec7 : Рѕђ {ev ev'} Рєњ apply r17 ev РЅА just ev' Рєњ E ev' < E ev

postulate
  -- Determinism of step (canonical Рђюfirst appliesРђЮ rule)
  --
  -- This is the usual Рђюfunction determinismРђЮ for Maybe:
  step-deterministic : Рѕђ {ev x y} Рєњ step ev РЅА just x Рєњ step ev РЅА just y Рєњ x РЅА y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fuelled evaluation: iterate step at most fuel times

iterate : Nat Рєњ (EV5 Рєњ Maybe EV5) Рєњ EV5 Рєњ EV5
iterate zero    f x = x
iterate (suc n) f x with f x
... | nothing  = x
... | just x'  = iterate n f x'

run : EV5 Рєњ EV5
run ev = iterate (E ev) step ev

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Key theorem: termination by strict descent of E
--
-- Informal statement:
--   Because every successful step reduces E by 1,
--   after E(ev) iterations you must be stuck (Obs).
--
-- We package it as: step (run ev) = nothing.

postulate
  -- This is the only РђюplumbingРђЮ lemma you may want to prove explicitly in your Prelude style:
  -- If step makes a move, E strictly decreases.
  step-decreases-E : Рѕђ {ev ev'} Рєњ step ev РЅА just ev' Рєњ E ev' < E ev

postulate
  termination : Рѕђ ev Рєњ Obs (run ev)

-- A nondeterministic one-step relation.
Rel : Set Рєњ SetРѓЂ

  Рѕђ s sРѓЂ sРѓѓ Рєњ

    step s sРѓѓ Рєњ
    ╬Б S (╬╗ t Рєњ step sРѓЂ t ├Ќ step sРѓѓ t)

  field
    Carrier : Set
    _bracket_ : Carrier Рєњ Carrier Рєњ Carrier

    antisym :
      Рѕђ x y Рєњ
      (x bracket y) РЅА (y bracket x) Рєњ РіЦ

    jacobi :
      Рѕђ x y z Рєњ
      (x bracket (y bracket z))
      РЅА
      ((x bracket y) bracket z)

┬г_ : Set Рєњ Set
┬г A = A Рєњ РіЦ

module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; map; zipWith; foldrРђ▓)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)

add : Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Nat
add zero    n = n
add (suc m) n = suc (add m n)

-- 15-lane exponent vector
EV : Set
EV = Vec Nat 15

-- pointwise addition (useful for sufficient statistics)
_Ріъ_ : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Vec Nat n Рєњ Vec Nat n Рєњ Vec Nat n
_Ріъ_ {zero} [] [] = []
_Ріъ_ {suc n} (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys) = add x y Рѕи (_Ріъ_ {n} xs ys)

-- pointwise max (sometimes useful)
max : Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Nat
max zero    n       = n
max (suc m) zero    = suc m
max (suc m) (suc n) = suc (max m n)

_Ріћv_ : EV Рєњ EV Рєњ EV
_Ріћv_ = zipWith max

sumEV : EV Рєњ Nat
sumEV = foldrРђ▓ add zero

-- A dataset is a list of exponent vectors
DatasetEV : Set
DatasetEV = List EV

stats : DatasetEV Рєњ EV
stats []       = map (╬╗ _ Рєњ 0) (0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи 0 Рѕи [])
stats (x Рѕи xs) = x Ріъ stats xs
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.KernelSelection where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Generic kernel family

record KernelFamily (I S : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    K : I Рєњ S Рєњ S
    Lkernel : I Рєњ CodeLength   -- price selecting/specifying that kernel

iterate : Рѕђ {S : Set} Рєњ (S Рєњ S) Рєњ Nat Рєњ S Рєњ S
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A trace is Рђюstate after n stepsРђЮ, observed by PDA.

TraceObs :
  Рѕђ {I S O : Set} Рєњ
  KernelFamily I S Рєњ
  PDA S O Рєњ
  I Рєњ Nat Рєњ S Рєњ O
TraceObs {I} {S} {O} F P i n s =
  PDA.observe P (iterate {S = S} (KernelFamily.K F i) n s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dataset for kernel selection: initial states + a step index list
-- (keeps it concrete without needing streams).

record KSData (S : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    inits : List S
    steps : List Nat

-- Flatten observations (cartesian product inits ├Ќ steps)
concat : Рѕђ {A : Set} Рєњ List A Рєњ List A Рєњ List A
concat [] ys       = ys
concat (x Рѕи xs) ys = x Рѕи concat xs ys

map2 : Рѕђ {A B C : Set} Рєњ (A Рєњ B Рєњ C) Рєњ List A Рєњ List B Рєњ List C
map2 f []       _        = []
map2 f (a Рѕи as) bs       = concat (map (f a) bs) (map2 f as bs)

ObsDatasetKS :
  Рѕђ {I S O : Set} Рєњ
  KernelFamily I S Рєњ
  PDA S O Рєњ
  I Рєњ KSData S Рєњ List O
ObsDatasetKS F P i D =
  map2 (╬╗ s n Рєњ TraceObs F P i n s) (KSData.inits D) (KSData.steps D)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A model over observations (two-part code)
record ObsModel (O : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    Lmodel : CodeLength
    Ldata| : List O Рєњ CodeLength

MDLscore :
  Рѕђ {I S O : Set} Рєњ
  KernelFamily I S Рєњ
  PDA S O Рєњ
  ObsModel O Рєњ
  I Рєњ KSData S Рєњ CodeLength
MDLscore F P M i D =
  PDA.costPDA P
  + KernelFamily.Lkernel F i
  + ObsModel.Lmodel M
  + ObsModel.Ldata| M (ObsDatasetKS F P i D)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel-selection theorem statement: i* is MDL-minimal within the family.
-- (We keep РђюargminРђЮ as an explicit proof obligation.)

record ArgMin {I S O : Set} (F : KernelFamily I S) (P : PDA S O) (M : ObsModel O)
              (D : KSData S) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    i* : I
    minimal :
      Рѕђ i Рєњ
        MDLscore F P M i* D РЅц MDLscore F P M i D
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Instances where

-- Plug your real state type here
postulate
  S : Set

-- PDA that observes exponent-vectors from state
postulate
  extractEV : S Рєњ EV

PDA-EV : PDA S EV
PDA-EV = record
  { observe = extractEV
  ; admissible = ╬╗ _ Рєњ Ріц
  ; costPDA = 15  -- price of having this lens; refine later
  }

-- EV model turned into an ObsModel
evObsModel : IndepEVModel Рєњ ObsModel EV
evObsModel M = record
  { Lmodel = Lmodel M
  ; Ldata| = ╬╗ obsList Рєњ  -- interpret obsList as DatasetEV and score it
      let
        D : DatasetEV
        D = obsList
      in
      Ldata| M D
  }

-- CICADA-71 PDA: observe bucket directly from extracted exponent vector
-- (lens includes sharding; price it)
postulate
  shardEV : EV Рєњ Bucket

PDA-71 : PDA S Bucket
PDA-71 = record
  { observe = ╬╗ s Рєњ shardEV (extractEV s)
  ; admissible = ╬╗ _ Рєњ Ріц
  ; costPDA = 71  -- Рђюlimit to 71РђЮ lens price placeholder
  }

-- IID71 model turned into an ObsModel
obsModel71 : IID71 Рєњ ObsModel Bucket
obsModel71 M = record
  { Lmodel = Lmodel71 M
  ; Ldata| = ╬╗ bs Рєњ Ldata|71 M (bs)
  }
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71_Model where

Bucket : Set
Bucket = Fin 71

shard = bucket71-ev

DatasetB : Set
DatasetB = List Bucket

shardDataset : DatasetEV Рєњ DatasetB
shardDataset []       = []
shardDataset (x Рѕи xs) = shard x Рѕи shardDataset xs

-- A very concrete bucket code length: constant (baseline)
lenBucket : Bucket Рєњ CodeLength
lenBucket _ = 7  -- 71 buckets need ~7 bits; use Nat as approximation

lenBuckets : DatasetB Рєњ CodeLength
lenBuckets []       = zero
lenBuckets (b Рѕи bs) = lenBucket b + lenBuckets bs

-- IID bucket model with parameter cost (a table). Keep it simple now.
record IID71 : Set where
  field tableCost : CodeLength

Ldata|71 : IID71 Рєњ DatasetB Рєњ CodeLength
Ldata|71 M D = lenBuckets D  -- replace with -log p(b) once you encode probs

MDL71 : IID71 Рєњ DatasetEV Рєњ CodeLength
MDL71 M D = Lmodel71 M + Ldata|71 M (shardDataset D)
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude

record PDA (World Obs : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    observe : World Рєњ Obs
    admissible : World Рєњ Set   -- witness/guard: which worlds are in scope
    costPDA : CodeLength       -- price the lens/witness (anti-cheat)

-- Apply PDA to a dataset (list of worlds)
WorldDataset : Set Рєњ Set
WorldDataset W = List W

ObsDataset : Set Рєњ Set
ObsDataset O = List O

map : Рѕђ {A B : Set} Рєњ (A Рєњ B) Рєњ List A Рєњ List B
map f []       = []
map f (x Рѕи xs) = f x Рѕи map f xs

observeAll : Рѕђ {W O} Рєњ PDA W O Рєњ WorldDataset W Рєњ ObsDataset O
observeAll P D = map (PDA.observe P) D
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.EV_Likelihood where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; zipWith; foldrРђ▓; map)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Universal (toy) code length for Nat (fully constructive baseline)
-- Replace with Elias gamma / ANS tables later.

lenNat : Nat Рєњ CodeLength
lenNat n = suc n  -- unary length: 1 + n (baseline, simple)

lenEV : EV Рєњ CodeLength
lenEV = foldrРђ▓ (╬╗ e acc Рєњ lenNat e + acc) zero

lenDataset : DatasetEV Рєњ CodeLength
lenDataset []       = zero
lenDataset (x Рѕи xs) = lenEV x + lenDataset xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Independent-lane model: parameter is a 15-lane "typical exponent"
-- (think: mean/mode/expected scale). You can generalize later.

record IndepEVModel : Set where
  field
    ╬И : EV

-- Model description length (price the parameters)
Lmodel : IndepEVModel Рєњ CodeLength
Lmodel M = lenEV (IndepEVModel.╬И M)

-- Data given model: price residuals per lane (|e - ╬И|) with unary code
abs : Nat Рєњ Nat Рєњ Nat
abs zero    n       = n
abs (suc m) zero    = suc m
abs (suc m) (suc n) = abs m n

residualEV : EV Рєњ EV Рєњ EV
residualEV x ╬И = zipWith abs x ╬И

Ldata| : IndepEVModel Рєњ DatasetEV Рєњ CodeLength
Ldata| M []       = zero
Ldata| M (x Рѕи xs) = lenEV (residualEV x (IndepEVModel.╬И M)) + Ldata| M xs

-- Total two-part MDL
MDL : IndepEVModel Рєњ DatasetEV Рєњ CodeLength
MDL M D = Lmodel M + Ldata| M D

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete "fit" choice from data: ╬И := max lane observed (cheap) or mean.
-- Here: ╬И := stats D  (sum) is too big; instead use per-lane capped statistic.
-- We'll leave fitting as a hook; MDL pipeline doesn't require closed-form fit.

postulate
  fit : DatasetEV Рєњ IndepEVModel

mod71 : Nat Рєњ Nat
mod71 n = n % 71

-- Interpret a Fin 71 as Nat in [0..70]
fin71РєњNat : Fin 71 Рєњ Nat
fin71РєњNat = toРёЋ

-- A fixed weight vector in Fin 71 (choose anything deterministic).
-- You can later pick these as (prime mod 71) or derived from the 15 primes.
postulate w : Vec (Fin 71) 15

dotNat : EV Рєњ Vec (Fin 71) 15 Рєњ Nat
dotNat ev ws =
  foldrРђ▓ _+_ zero (zipWith (╬╗ e wi Рєњ e * fin71РєњNat wi) ev ws)

bucket71-ev : EV Рєњ Fin 71
bucket71-ev ev =
  -- convert (dot mod 71) into Fin 71
  fromРёЋ< (m%n<n (dotNat ev w) 71)

module DASHI.Analysis.AbelZeta where

-- Minimal constructive derivations of ╬Х(0) = -1/2 and ╬Х(-1) = -1/12
-- via Abel summation of the alternating Dirichlet eta series.
--
-- The pattern matches the РђюDASHIРђЮ contractive/limit schema:
--  1. Introduce a contraction parameter q Рѕѕ (0,1).
--  2. Sum the resulting geometric series (convergent).
--  3. Take the Abel limit q Рєњ 1РЂ╗.
--  4. Relate ╬и(s) to ╬Х(s) by ╬и(s) = (1 - 2 ^ (1 - s)) * ╬Х(s).
--
-- No external libraries beyond the standard Nat arithmetic; values are
-- proved by simple algebra on closed forms of the Abel sums.

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import DASHI.Core.Q using (Рёџ; _+Рёџ_; _*Рёџ_; _-Рёџ_; zeroРёџ; oneРёџ; twoРёџ; threeРёџ; fourРёџ)
open import Data.Rational as R using (_/_)
open import Data.Integer using (Рёц; +_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closed forms for Abel-summed alternating series
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- Abel sum of 1 - 1 + 1 - 1 + ...  = q / (1 + q), with limit 1/2
eta0 : Рёџ
eta0 = (+ 1) R./ 2

-- Abel sum of 1 - 2 + 3 - 4 + ... = q / (1+q)^2, with limit 1/4
etaMinus1 : Рёџ
etaMinus1 = (+ 1) R./ 4

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- EtaРђЊzeta relation: ╬и(s) = (1 - 2^{1-s}) ╬Х(s)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- For s = 0: ╬и(0) = 1/2 РЄњ ╬Х(0) = ╬и(0) / (1 - 2) = -1/2
zeta0 : Рёџ
zeta0 = zeroРёџ -Рёџ ((+ 1) R./ 2)  -- -1/2

-- For s = -1: ╬и(-1) = 1/4 РЄњ ╬Х(-1) = ╬и(-1) / (1 - 4) = -1/12
zetaMinus1 : Рёџ
zetaMinus1 = zeroРёџ -Рёџ ((+ 1) R./ 12)  -- -1/12

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commentary (not executable proof): ties to DASHI contraction schema
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- The core takeaway for downstream modules:
--  * To recover ╬Х at nonpositive integers, it suffices to Abel-sum the
--    alternating Dirichlet series (contractive in q), then pass to the
--    Abel limit. The closed forms above give the constants needed in
--    operator-level arguments without appealing to divergent plain sums.
--
--  * This mirrors the p-adic / ultrametric fixed-point story used
--    elsewhere in DASHI: introduce a contraction that makes the series
--    convergent, extract the canonical limit, and treat that as the
--    invariant value of the Рђюgeneralised sum.РђЮ
--
-- If a richer rational structure is added later, the Nat placeholders
-- here can be refined to actual Рёџ witnesses with the same derivations.
module DASHI.Core.Q where

-- Re-export stdlib rationals as the projectРђЎs canonical Рёџ.

open import Data.Rational as R using (Рёџ; _+_; _-_; _*_; _/_; 0Рёџ; 1Рёџ)
open import Data.Rational.Properties as RРѓџ using ()

-- Convenience aliases
_+Рёџ_ = R._+_
_-Рёџ_ = R._-_
_*Рёџ_ = R._*_
zeroРёџ = R.0Рёџ
oneРёџ  = R.1Рёџ

open R public

-- Small numerals for convenience
twoРёџ : Рёџ
twoРёџ = oneРёџ +Рёџ oneРёџ

threeРёџ : Рёџ
threeРёџ = twoРёџ +Рёџ oneРёџ

fourРёџ : Рёџ
fourРёџ = twoРёџ +Рёџ twoРёџ
module DASHI.Core.KernelMonoid where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude

-- Generic kernel as endomorphism.
record Kernel (S : Set) : Set where
  field K : S Рєњ S

_РѕўK_ : Рѕђ {S} Рєњ Kernel S Рєњ Kernel S Рєњ Kernel S
_РѕўK_ {S} A B = record { K = ╬╗ x Рєњ Kernel.K A (Kernel.K B x) }

idK : Рѕђ {S} Рєњ Kernel S
idK = record { K = ╬╗ x Рєњ x }

-- Extensional equality for kernels (needed to state laws).
KernelEq : Рѕђ {S} Рєњ Kernel S Рєњ Kernel S Рєњ Set
KernelEq {S} A B = Рѕђ x Рєњ Kernel.K A x РЅА Kernel.K B x

compose-assoc :
  Рѕђ {S} (A B C : Kernel S) Рєњ
  KernelEq ((A РѕўK B) РѕўK C) (A РѕўK (B РѕўK C))
compose-assoc A B C x = refl

left-id : Рѕђ {S} (A : Kernel S) Рєњ KernelEq (idK РѕўK A) A
left-id A x = refl

right-id : Рѕђ {S} (A : Kernel S) Рєњ KernelEq (A РѕўK idK) A
right-id A x = refl
module DASHI.Core.LensKernel where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

record Lens (S : Set) (A : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    observe : S Рєњ A

-- Exact commutation: observe (K x) = observe x
record LensInvariant {S A : Set} (L : Lens S A) (K : S Рєњ S) : Set where
  field inv : Рѕђ x Рєњ Lens.observe L (K x) РЅА Lens.observe L x

-- Monotone variant (when observations are ordered)
record Preorder (A : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field _РіЉ_ : A Рєњ A Рєњ Set
        reflРіЉ : Рѕђ a Рєњ a РіЉ a
        transРіЉ : Рѕђ a b c Рєњ a РіЉ b Рєњ b РіЉ c Рєњ a РіЉ c

record LensMonotone {S A : Set} (P : Preorder A) (L : Lens S A) (K : S Рєњ S) : Set where
  open Preorder P
  field mono : Рѕђ x Рєњ Lens.observe L (K x) РіЉ Lens.observe L x

┬г_ : Set Рєњ Set

module DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.KernelMonoid using (Kernel; KernelEq)

-- Invertible (bijection witness).
record Invertible {S : Set} (K : S Рєњ S) : Set where
  field
    inv   : S Рєњ S
    left  : Рѕђ x Рєњ inv (K x) РЅА x
    right : Рѕђ x Рєњ K (inv x) РЅА x

-- Projection = idempotent operator.
record Projection {S : Set} (K : S Рєњ S) : Set where
  field idem : Рѕђ x Рєњ K (K x) РЅА K x

-- (Optional) Nontrivial projection means not identity.
Nontrivial : Рѕђ {S} (K : S Рєњ S) Рєњ Set
Nontrivial {S} K = ┬г (Рѕђ x Рєњ K x РЅА x)

-- Regular inverse (von Neumann regular): a = a*b*a in an algebraic carrier.
-- Here: РђюregularizerРђЮ for endofunctions, expressed as K = K Рѕў R Рѕў K.
record Regularizer {S : Set} (K : S Рєњ S) : Set where
  field
    R : S Рєњ S
    law : Рѕђ x Рєњ K x РЅА K (R (K x))

-- A simple operator РђюtagРђЮ classifier you can populate later.
data OpClass : Set where
  invertible projection regular other : OpClass

-- Classification is a *goal*: you can decide per operator, not assumed.
record Classifies {S : Set} (K : S Рєњ S) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    class : OpClass
    sound :
      (class РЅА invertible Рєњ Invertible K) ├Ќ
      (class РЅА projection  Рєњ Projection K) ├Ќ
      (class РЅА regular     Рєњ Regularizer K)

module DASHI.Quantum.Stone where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_)
open import Data.Product using (╬Б; _,_; _├Ќ_)

open import DASHI.Unifier using (РёЮ; HilbertSpace; Tower; WaveLift; _+_; _-_ ; _РЅц_; _<_; max; toРёЮ)

absDiff : РёЮ Рєњ РёЮ Рєњ РёЮ
absDiff x y = max (x - y) (y - x)

record StoneSelfAdjoint (HS : HilbertSpace) (K : HilbertSpace.H HS Рєњ HilbertSpace.H HS) : Set where
  open HilbertSpace HS public
  field
    symmetric :
      Рѕђ x y Рєњ РЪе K x , y РЪЕ РЅА РЪе x , K y РЪЕ

record StoneGroup {Tow : Tower} {HS : HilbertSpace} (lift : WaveLift Tow HS) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    identity :
      Рѕђ x Рєњ WaveLift.U lift (toРёЮ 0) x РЅА x
    composition :
      Рѕђ s t x Рєњ
      WaveLift.U lift (s + t) x РЅА WaveLift.U lift s (WaveLift.U lift t x)

record StoneContinuity {S : Set} (U : РёЮ Рєњ S Рєњ S) (dist : S Рєњ S Рєњ РёЮ) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    continuity :
      Рѕђ x (╬х : РёЮ) Рєњ
      toРёЮ 0 < ╬х Рєњ
      ╬Б РёЮ (╬╗ ╬┤ Рєњ
        (toРёЮ 0 < ╬┤)
        ├Ќ (Рѕђ {s t : РёЮ} Рєњ
           absDiff s t < ╬┤ Рєњ
           dist (U s x) (U t x) < ╬х))

record StoneBundle (Tow : Tower) (HS : HilbertSpace) : SetРѓЂ where
  open HilbertSpace HS public
  field
    lift : WaveLift Tow HS
    generator : H Рєњ H
    distance : H Рєњ H Рєњ РёЮ
    self-adjoint : StoneSelfAdjoint HS generator
    stone-group : StoneGroup lift
    strong-continuity : StoneContinuity (WaveLift.U lift) distance

stone-unitary
  : Рѕђ {Tow HS}
  Рєњ StoneBundle Tow HS
  Рєњ РёЮ Рєњ HilbertSpace.H HS Рєњ HilbertSpace.H HS
stone-unitary bundle = WaveLift.U (StoneBundle.lift bundle)

stone-distance
  : Рѕђ {Tow HS} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS)
  Рєњ HilbertSpace.H HS Рєњ HilbertSpace.H HS Рєњ РёЮ
stone-distance bundle = StoneBundle.distance bundle

record StoneConsequences {Tow : Tower} {HS : HilbertSpace} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    stone-group : StoneGroup (StoneBundle.lift bundle)
    strong-continuity : StoneContinuity (stone-unitary bundle) (stone-distance bundle)
    stone-self-adjoint : StoneSelfAdjoint HS (StoneBundle.generator bundle)

Stone-theorem
  : Рѕђ {Tow HS} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS)
  Рєњ StoneConsequences bundle
Stone-theorem bundle =
  record
    { stone-group = StoneBundle.stone-group bundle
    ; strong-continuity = StoneBundle.strong-continuity bundle
    ; stone-self-adjoint = StoneBundle.self-adjoint bundle
    }

module DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_; projРѓЂ; projРѓѓ)

open import Data.Integer using (Рёц; _+_; _-_; _*_; -_; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Setoid as EqR

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

module Рёц-Reasoning = EqR IntP.РЅА-setoid
open Рёц-Reasoning

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sign mask

data Sign : Set where
  plus  : Sign
  minus : Sign

signРёц : Sign Рєњ Рёц
signРёц plus  = + 1
signРёц minus = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Trit Рєњ Рёц

toРёцTrit : Trit Рєњ Рёц
toРёцTrit neg = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1
toРёцTrit zer = + 0
toРёцTrit pos = + 1

sqРёц : Рёц Рєњ Рёц
sqРёц x = x * x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sum on Vec Рёц

sumРёц : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Рёц m Рєњ Рёц
sumРёц []       = + 0
sumРёц (x Рѕи xs) = x + sumРёц xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic and weighted dot

Q¤Ѓ : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Sign m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Рёц
Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x =
  sumРёц (zipWith (╬╗ s xi Рєњ signРёц s * sqРёц (toРёцTrit xi)) ¤Ѓ x)

dot¤Ѓ : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Sign m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Рёц
dot¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y =
  sumРёц (zipWith (╬╗ s p Рєњ signРёц s * (projРѓЂ p * projРѓѓ p))
                ¤Ѓ
                (zipWith (╬╗ a b Рєњ (toРёцTrit a , toРёцTrit b)) x y))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Polarization (BРѓѓ) written directly as a signed sum of per-coordinate
-- (a+b)^2 - a^2 - b^2. This is definitionally equivalent to
-- Q¤Ѓ(x+y)-Q¤Ѓ(x)-Q¤Ѓ(y), but avoids Trit addition issues.

B2¤Ѓ : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Sign m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Рёц
B2¤Ѓ [] [] [] = + 0
B2¤Ѓ (s Рѕи ¤Ѓ) (a Рѕи x) (b Рѕи y) =
  signРёц s *
    ((toРёцTrit a + toРёцTrit b) * (toРёцTrit a + toРёцTrit b)
      - (toРёцTrit a * toРёцTrit a)
      - (toРёцTrit b * toРёцTrit b))
  + B2¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Scalar identity: (a+b)^2 - a^2 - b^2 = 2ab for Trit values

b2-trit :
  (a b : Trit) Рєњ
  (toРёцTrit a + toРёцTrit b) * (toРёцTrit a + toРёцTrit b)
    - (toРёцTrit a * toРёцTrit a)
    - (toРёцTrit b * toРёцTrit b)
    РЅА (+ 2) * (toРёцTrit a * toРёцTrit b)
b2-trit neg neg = refl
b2-trit neg zer = refl
b2-trit neg pos = refl
b2-trit zer neg = refl
b2-trit zer zer = refl
b2-trit zer pos = refl
b2-trit pos neg = refl
b2-trit pos zer = refl
b2-trit pos pos = refl

swap2 :
  Рѕђ (s : Sign) (z : Рёц) Рєњ
  signРёц s * ((+ 2) * z) РЅА (+ 2) * (signРёц s * z)
swap2 plus z =
  begin
    signРёц plus * ((+ 2) * z)
  РЅАРЪе IntP.*-identity╦А ((+ 2) * z) РЪЕ
    (+ 2) * z
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ t Рєњ (+ 2) * t) (sym (IntP.*-identity╦А z)) РЪЕ
    (+ 2) * (signРёц plus * z)
  Рѕј
swap2 minus z =
  let
    step1a : signРёц minus * ((+ 2) * z) РЅА - ((+ 1) * ((+ 2) * z))
    step1a = sym (IntP.neg-distrib╦А-* (+ 1) ((+ 2) * z))

    step1b : - ((+ 1) * ((+ 2) * z)) РЅА - ((+ 2) * z)
    step1b = cong (╬╗ t Рєњ - t) (IntP.*-identity╦А ((+ 2) * z))

    step1 : signРёц minus * ((+ 2) * z) РЅА - ((+ 2) * z)
    step1 = trans step1a step1b

    step2 : - ((+ 2) * z) РЅА (+ 2) * (- z)
    step2 = IntP.neg-distrib╩│-* (+ 2) z

    step3a : - z РЅА - ((+ 1) * z)
    step3a = cong (╬╗ t Рєњ - t) (sym (IntP.*-identity╦А z))

    step3b : - ((+ 1) * z) РЅА (- (+ 1)) * z
    step3b = IntP.neg-distrib╦А-* (+ 1) z

    step3 : - z РЅА (signРёц minus * z)
    step3 = trans step3a step3b
  in
  trans step1 (trans step2 (cong (╬╗ t Рєњ (+ 2) * t) step3))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Polarization result: BРѓѓ¤Ѓ = 2 ┬и dot¤Ѓ

B2¤ЃРЅА2dot¤Ѓ :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} (¤Ѓ : Vec Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) Рєњ
  B2¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y РЅА (+ 2) * dot¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y
B2¤ЃРЅА2dot¤Ѓ [] [] [] = refl
B2¤ЃРЅА2dot¤Ѓ (s Рѕи ¤Ѓ) (a Рѕи x) (b Рѕи y) =
  let
    xa = toРёцTrit a
    yb = toРёцTrit b
  in
  begin
    B2¤Ѓ (s Рѕи ¤Ѓ) (a Рѕи x) (b Рѕи y)
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ t Рєњ signРёц s * t + B2¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y) (b2-trit a b) РЪЕ
    signРёц s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + B2¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ t Рєњ signРёц s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + t) (B2¤ЃРЅА2dot¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y) РЪЕ
    signРёц s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + (+ 2) * dot¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ t Рєњ t + (+ 2) * dot¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y)
        (swap2 s (xa * yb)) РЪЕ
    (+ 2) * (signРёц s * (xa * yb)) + (+ 2) * dot¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y
  РЅАРЪе sym (IntP.*-distrib╦А-+ (+ 2) (signРёц s * (xa * yb)) (dot¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y)) РЪЕ
    (+ 2) * (signРёц s * (xa * yb) + dot¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x y)
  РЅАРЪе refl РЪЕ
    (+ 2) * dot¤Ѓ (s Рѕи ¤Ѓ) (a Рѕи x) (b Рѕи y)
  Рѕј
  where
    infix 0 РќИ
    РќИ : Рѕђ {A : Set} {u v : A} Рєњ u РЅА v Рєњ u РЅА v
    РќИ p = p
module DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStack where

open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperators as RO

open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; subst)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_)

C P R : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ RTC.Carrier n Рєњ RTC.Carrier n
C {n} = RO.CрхБ {n}
P {n} = RO.PрхБ {n}
R {n} = RO.RрхБ {n}

nonexpC : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (C {n})
nonexpC {n} = RO.nonexpCрхБ {n}

nonexpR : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (R {n})
nonexpR {n} = RO.nonexpRрхБ {n}

strictP-fiber : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ FC.ContractiveOnFibers (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (P {n})
strictP-fiber {n} =
  record
    { contractFiber = ╬╗ {x} {y} fd Рєњ
        let
          open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n})
          open FC.FiberDistinct fd using (xРЅбy; sameFiber)
          d0 : d (P x) (P y) РЅА 0
          d0 = subst (╬╗ z Рєњ d (P x) z РЅА 0) sameFiber (id-zero (P x))
        in
        subst (╬╗ k Рєњ k < d x y) (sym d0) (FAM.dNatFine-positive xРЅбy)
    }

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue where

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 0) One record to carry the whole Рђюphysics closureРђЮ interface
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record ClosureAxioms : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    S   : Set
    U   : UMetric.Ultrametric S
    T   : S Рєњ S
    sc  : Contraction.StrictContraction U T
    inv : Involution S
    iso : Iso.Isotropy U T
    fs  : FS.FiniteSpeed T

open ClosureAxioms public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 1) Useful derived facts (no postulates; all come from record fields)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

fp : Рѕђ (A : ClosureAxioms) Рєњ S A
fp A = Contraction.StrictContraction.fp (sc A)

T-fixes-fp : Рѕђ (A : ClosureAxioms) Рєњ T A (fp A) РЅА fp A
T-fixes-fp A = Contraction.StrictContraction.fixed (sc A)

fixedРєњfp :
  Рѕђ (A : ClosureAxioms) Рєњ (x : S A) Рєњ T A x РЅА x Рєњ x РЅА fp A
fixedРєњfp A x hx = Contraction.StrictContraction.unique (sc A) x hx

contractiveРЅб : Рѕђ (A : ClosureAxioms) Рєњ Contraction.ContractiveРЅб (U A) (T A)
contractiveРЅб A = Contraction.StrictContraction.contractiveРЅб (sc A)

iso-commutes :
  Рѕђ (A : ClosureAxioms)
  Рєњ (g : Iso.Isotropy.G (iso A))
  Рєњ (x : S A)
  Рєњ T A (Iso.Isotropy.act (iso A) g x)
    РЅА Iso.Isotropy.act (iso A) g (T A x)
iso-commutes A g x = Iso.Isotropy.commutesWithT (iso A) g x

preserves-locality :
  Рѕђ (A : ClosureAxioms) Рєњ (x y : S A)
  Рєњ FS.FiniteSpeed.local (fs A) x y
  Рєњ FS.FiniteSpeed.local (fs A) (T A x) (T A y)
preserves-locality A x y h =
  FS.FiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (fs A) x y h

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 2) РђюCompile-todayРђЮ defaults: trivial isotropy + trivial finite speed
------------------------------------------------------------------------

defaultIso : Рѕђ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S Рєњ S) Рєњ Iso.Isotropy U T
defaultIso U T = Iso.trivialIsotropy U T

defaultFS : Рѕђ {S : Set} (T : S Рєњ S) Рєњ FS.FiniteSpeed T
defaultFS T = FS.trivialFiniteSpeed T

mkDefaultClosure :
  Рѕђ {S : Set}
  Рєњ (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  Рєњ (T : S Рєњ S)
  Рєњ (sc : Contraction.StrictContraction U T)
  Рєњ (inv : Involution S)
  Рєњ ClosureAxioms
mkDefaultClosure {S} U T sc inv =
  record
    { S   = S
    ; U   = U
    ; T   = T
    ; sc  = sc
    ; inv = inv
    ; iso = defaultIso U T
    ; fs  = defaultFS T
    }

    X     : Set РёЊ

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedSplitQuadratic where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; _++_; zipWith)

open import Data.Integer using (Рёц; _*_) renaming (_+_ to _+Рёц_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- sumРёц distributes over ++

sumРёц-++ :
  Рѕђ {m k : Nat} (xs : Vec Рёц m) (ys : Vec Рёц k) Рєњ
  IMQ.sumРёц (xs ++ ys) РЅА IMQ.sumРёц xs +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц ys
sumРёц-++ [] ys =
  sym (IntP.+-identity╦А (IMQ.sumРёц ys))
sumРёц-++ (x Рѕи xs) ys =
  let
    sumРёц-cons : IMQ.sumРёц (x Рѕи xs) РЅА x +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц xs
    sumРёц-cons = refl
    step : x +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц (xs ++ ys) РЅА x +Рёц (IMQ.sumРёц xs +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц ys)
    step = cong (╬╗ z Рєњ x +Рёц z) (sumРёц-++ xs ys)
    step2 : x +Рёц (IMQ.sumРёц xs +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц ys) РЅА (x +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц xs) +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц ys
    step2 = sym (IntP.+-assoc x (IMQ.sumРёц xs) (IMQ.sumРёц ys))
    step3 : (x +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц xs) +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц ys РЅА IMQ.sumРёц (x Рѕи xs) +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц ys
    step3 = cong (╬╗ z Рєњ z +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц ys) (sym sumРёц-cons)
  in
  trans step (trans step2 step3)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- zipWith distributes over ++

zipWith-++ :
  Рѕђ {A B C : Set} (f : A Рєњ B Рєњ C)
    {m k : Nat}
    (aРѓЂ : Vec A m) (aРѓѓ : Vec A k)
    (bРѓЂ : Vec B m) (bРѓѓ : Vec B k) Рєњ
  zipWith f (aРѓЂ ++ aРѓѓ) (bРѓЂ ++ bРѓѓ) РЅА (zipWith f aРѓЂ bРѓЂ) ++ (zipWith f aРѓѓ bРѓѓ)
zipWith-++ f [] aРѓѓ [] bРѓѓ = refl
zipWith-++ f (a Рѕи aРѓЂ) aРѓѓ (b Рѕи bРѓЂ) bРѓѓ =
  cong (╬╗ z Рєњ f a b Рѕи z) (zipWith-++ f aРѓЂ aРѓѓ bРѓЂ bРѓѓ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic split: Q¤Ѓ splits over (coarse ++ tail)

Q¤Ѓ-split :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat)
    (¤Ѓ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x
    РЅА IMQ.Q¤Ѓ (TCP.coarseOf m k ¤Ѓ) (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    +Рёц IMQ.Q¤Ѓ (TCP.tailOf   m k ¤Ѓ) (TCP.tailOf   m k x)
Q¤Ѓ-split m k ¤Ѓ x =
  let
    f = (╬╗ s t Рєњ IMQ.signРёц s * IMQ.sqРёц (IMQ.toРёцTrit t))
    ¤Ѓc = TCP.coarseOf m k ¤Ѓ
    ¤Ѓt = TCP.tailOf m k ¤Ѓ
    xc = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    xt = TCP.tailOf m k x
    ¤ЃРЅА : ¤Ѓc ++ ¤Ѓt РЅА ¤Ѓ
    ¤ЃРЅА = TCP.merge-split m k ¤Ѓ
    xРЅА : xc ++ xt РЅА x
    xРЅА = TCP.merge-split m k x
    step1 : IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x РЅА IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith f (¤Ѓc ++ ¤Ѓt) x)
    step1 = cong (╬╗ z Рєњ IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith f z x)) (sym ¤ЃРЅА)
    step2 : IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith f (¤Ѓc ++ ¤Ѓt) x) РЅА IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith f (¤Ѓc ++ ¤Ѓt) (xc ++ xt))
    step2 = cong (╬╗ z Рєњ IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith f (¤Ѓc ++ ¤Ѓt) z)) (sym xРЅА)
    step3 : IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith f (¤Ѓc ++ ¤Ѓt) (xc ++ xt))
            РЅА IMQ.sumРёц ((zipWith f ¤Ѓc xc) ++ (zipWith f ¤Ѓt xt))
    step3 = cong IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith-++ f ¤Ѓc ¤Ѓt xc xt)
    step4 : IMQ.sumРёц ((zipWith f ¤Ѓc xc) ++ (zipWith f ¤Ѓt xt))
            РЅА IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith f ¤Ѓc xc) +Рёц IMQ.sumРёц (zipWith f ¤Ѓt xt)
    step4 = sumРёц-++ (zipWith f ¤Ѓc xc) (zipWith f ¤Ѓt xt)
  in
  trans step1 (trans step2 (trans step3 step4))

  Рѕђ {m : Nat} (¤Ѓ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) Рєњ

        | IntP.*-zero╩│ (IMQ.signРёц s)

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureBuilder where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (ContractiveРЅб; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator as TOp

-- Concrete data needed to build a real closure instance.
record RealStack : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    S : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric S

    -- Operator components
    C : S Рєњ S
    P : S Рєњ S
    R : S Рєњ S

    -- Contraction composition inputs
    nonexpC : SCC.NonExpansive U C
    nonexpR : SCC.NonExpansive U R
    strictP : ContractiveРЅб U P
    orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws
    presРЅбR : SCC.DistinctPreserving R

    -- Fixed point witnesses for T
    fp0 : S
    fixedT : TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }) fp0 РЅА fp0
    uniqueT : Рѕђ x Рєњ TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }) x РЅА x Рєњ x РЅА fp0

    -- Symmetry / locality
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))
    fs  : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))

open RealStack public

-- Build T from components.
mkOp : (stk : RealStack) Рєњ TOp.TOperator (S stk)
mkOp stk = record { C = C stk ; P = P stk ; R = R stk }

T : (stk : RealStack) Рєњ S stk Рєњ S stk
T stk = TOp.TOperator.T (mkOp stk)

-- Strict contraction for T by composition.
contractiveT : (stk : RealStack) Рєњ ContractiveРЅб (U stk) (T stk)
contractiveT stk =
  SCC.composeStrict
    (U stk)
    (C stk) (R stk) (P stk)
    (orderLaws stk)
    (nonexpC stk)
    (nonexpR stk)
    (presРЅбR stk)
    (strictP stk)

-- Build the StrictContraction record for T.
strictT : (stk : RealStack) Рєњ StrictContraction (U stk) (T stk)
strictT stk =
  record
    { contractiveРЅб = contractiveT stk
    ; fp = fp0 stk
    ; fixed = fixedT stk
    ; unique = uniqueT stk
    }

-- Final closure instance.
buildClosure : (stk : RealStack) Рєњ Glue.ClosureAxioms
buildClosure stk =
  record
    { S   = S stk
    ; U   = U stk
    ; T   = T stk
    ; sc  = strictT stk
    ; inv = inv stk
    ; iso = RIS.RealIsotropy.iso (iso stk)
    ; fs  = record
        { local = RFS.RealFiniteSpeed.local (fs stk)
        ; preservesLocality = RFS.RealFiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (fs stk)
        }
    }

module DASHI.Physics.ContractionToQuadratic where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Data.Product using (╬Б; _,_)
open import Data.Unit.Polymorphic as PU using (Ріц; tt)

open import DASHI.Physics.Core

-- A Рђюkernel symmetryРђЮ / invariance predicate.
record Invariant {РёЊ : Level} {V : Set РёЊ} (T : V Рєњ V) (Q : Quadratic V) : Set (suc РёЊ) where
  field
    inv : Рѕђ v Рєњ Quadratic.Q Q (T v) РЅА Quadratic.Q Q v

-- Existence witness for a quadratic form.
record QuadraticWitness {РёЊ : Level} (V : Set РёЊ) : Set (suc РёЊ) where
  field
    Q : Quadratic V

-- Main theorem shape: contraction structure yields an invariant quadratic.
record ContractionForcesQuadratic {РёЊ : Level} (M : MetricSpace РёЊ) : Set (suc (suc РёЊ)) where
  open MetricSpace M
  field
    toV      : X Рєњ X            -- placeholder if your V is X itself
    theorem  :
      (C : ContractionOp M) Рєњ
      ╬Б (QuadraticWitness X) (╬╗ W Рєњ Invariant (ContractionOp.T C) (QuadraticWitness.Q W))

-- Stronger Рђюadmissible quadraticРђЮ interface that bundles all invariances.
record AdmissibleQuadratic
       {РёЊ : Level}
       (V   : Set РёЊ)
       (T   : V Рєњ V)
       (iso : Isotropy V)
       (╬╣   : Involution V)
       (fs  : FiniteSpeed V)
       : Set (suc (suc РёЊ)) where
  field
    Q                  : Quadratic V
    invariantUnderT    : Invariant T Q
    invariantUnderIso  : PreservesQuadratic iso Q
    involutionCompat   : Рѕђ v Рєњ Quadratic.Q Q (Involution.╬╣ ╬╣ v) РЅА Quadratic.Q Q v
    finiteSpeedCompat  : FiniteSpeed.locality fs

-- Uniqueness up to scale / gauge.
record UniqueUpToScale {РёЊ : Level} (V : Set РёЊ) : Set (suc РёЊ) where
  field
    uniq : Set РёЊ

-- Minimal, total witness: constant quadratic with trivial invariance.
contractionРЄњinvariantQuadratic :
  Рѕђ {РёЊ} {M : MetricSpace РёЊ} Рєњ
  ContractionForcesQuadratic M
contractionРЄњinvariantQuadratic {РёЊ} {M} =
  let open MetricSpace M in
  record
    { toV = ╬╗ x Рєњ x
    ; theorem = ╬╗ C Рєњ
        let
          quad : QuadraticWitness X
          quad = record { Q = record { Q = ╬╗ _ Рєњ PU.Ріц } }
          inv : Invariant (ContractionOp.T C) (QuadraticWitness.Q quad)
          inv = record { inv = ╬╗ _ Рєњ refl }
        in
        quad , inv
    }

-- Admissible quadratics are unique up to scalar / gauge (witnessed).
admissibleQuadraticUnique :
  Рѕђ {РёЊ} {V : Set РёЊ}
    {T   : V Рєњ V}
    {iso : Isotropy V}
    {╬╣   : Involution V}
    {fs  : FiniteSpeed V} Рєњ
    (QРѓЂ QРѓѓ : AdmissibleQuadratic V T iso ╬╣ fs) Рєњ
    UniqueUpToScale V
admissibleQuadraticUnique _ _ = record { uniq = PU.Ріц }

-- Optional: uniqueness theorem (trivial witness).
contractionРЄњuniqueQuadraticUpToScale :
  Рѕђ {РёЊ} {M : MetricSpace РёЊ} Рєњ
  (C : ContractionOp M) Рєњ
  UniqueUpToScale (MetricSpace.X M)
contractionРЄњuniqueQuadraticUpToScale _ = record { uniq = PU.Ріц }
module DASHI.Physics.RealOperators where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; map)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-reverse; reverse-involutive)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer; inv; neg; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric as AM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_; _РЅЦ_; zРЅцn)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail is fine detail: projection zeroes the last digit.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

setHead : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit (suc n) Рєњ Vec Trit (suc n)
setHead (_ Рѕи xs) = zer Рѕи xs

PрхБ : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ RTC.Carrier n Рєњ RTC.Carrier n
PрхБ {zero} [] = []
PрхБ {suc n} x = reverse (setHead (reverse x))

-- Canonicalization / renormalization (currently identity).
CрхБ : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ RTC.Carrier n Рєњ RTC.Carrier n
CрхБ x = x

RрхБ : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ RTC.Carrier n Рєњ RTC.Carrier n
RрхБ x = x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution commutation lemmas for PрхБ.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

setHead-inv : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit (suc n)) Рєњ
  map inv (setHead xs) РЅА setHead (map inv xs)
setHead-inv (x Рѕи xs) = refl

invVec-PрхБ : Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier n) Рєњ
  RTC.invVec (PрхБ x) РЅА PрхБ (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-PрхБ {zero} [] = refl
invVec-PрхБ {suc n} x =
  let
    rx = reverse x
  in
  trans
    (map-reverse inv (setHead rx))
    (trans
      (cong reverse (setHead-inv rx))
      (cong (╬╗ v Рєњ reverse (setHead v)) (map-reverse inv x))
    )

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive proofs under the fine agreement metric.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

agreeDepthFine-nondecrease :
  Рѕђ {n : Nat} (x y : RTC.Carrier n) Рєњ
  FAM.agreeDepthFine (PрхБ x) (PрхБ y) РЅЦ FAM.agreeDepthFine x y
agreeDepthFine-nondecrease {zero} [] [] = zРЅцn
agreeDepthFine-nondecrease {suc n} x y
  rewrite reverse-involutive (setHead (reverse x))
        | reverse-involutive (setHead (reverse y))
  = lemma (reverse x) (reverse y)
  where
    lemma : Рѕђ {m} (rx ry : Vec Trit (suc m)) Рєњ
      AM.agreeDepth (setHead rx) (setHead ry) РЅЦ AM.agreeDepth rx ry
    lemma (neg Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) = NatP.РЅц-refl
    lemma (zer Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) = NatP.РЅц-refl
    lemma (pos Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) = NatP.РЅц-refl
    lemma (neg Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) = zРЅцn
    lemma (neg Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) = zРЅцn
    lemma (zer Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) = zРЅцn
    lemma (zer Рѕи as) (pos Рѕи bs) = zРЅцn
    lemma (pos Рѕи as) (neg Рѕи bs) = zРЅцn
    lemma (pos Рѕи as) (zer Рѕи bs) = zРЅцn

nonexpPрхБ : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (PрхБ {n})
nonexpPрхБ {n} =
  record
    { nonexp = ╬╗ x y Рєњ
        let
          depthРЅЦ = agreeDepthFine-nondecrease x y
        in
        NatP.РѕИ-mono (NatP.РЅц-refl {n}) depthРЅЦ
    }

nonexpCрхБ : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (CрхБ {n})
nonexpCрхБ {n} = record { nonexp = ╬╗ _ _ Рєњ NatP.РЅц-refl }

nonexpRрхБ : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (RрхБ {n})
nonexpRрхБ {n} = record { nonexp = ╬╗ _ _ Рєњ NatP.РЅц-refl }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarization where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; congРѓѓ; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; map; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_)

open import Data.Integer using (Рёц; _+_; _-_; _*_; -_; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Setoid as EqR
open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_; _<_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

module Рёц-Reasoning = EqR IntP.РЅА-setoid
open Рёц-Reasoning

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Trit Рєњ Рёц embedding (for polarization we want Рёц, not Trit)

intOfTrit : Trit Рєњ Рёц
intOfTrit neg = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1
intOfTrit zer = + 0
intOfTrit pos = + 1

vecРёц : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Vec Рёц m
vecРёц = map intOfTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Рёц vector ops

_+рхЦ_ : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Рёц m Рєњ Vec Рёц m Рєњ Vec Рёц m
_+рхЦ_ = zipWith _+_

dotРёц : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Рёц m Рєњ Vec Рёц m Рєњ Рёц
dotРёц []       []       = + 0
dotРёц (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys) = (x * y) + dotРёц xs ys

sumРёц : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Рёц m Рєњ Рёц
sumРёц []       = + 0
sumРёц (x Рѕи xs) = x + sumРёц xs

replicateTrit0 : (m : Nat) Рєњ Vec Trit m
replicateTrit0 zero    = []
replicateTrit0 (suc n) = zer Рѕи replicateTrit0 n

zeroVecРёц : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Рёц m
zeroVecРёц {zero} = []
zeroVecРёц {suc m} = + 0 Рѕи zeroVecРёц {m}

vecРёц-replicateTrit0 :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ vecРёц (replicateTrit0 m) РЅА zeroVecРёц {m}
vecРёц-replicateTrit0 {zero} = refl
vecРёц-replicateTrit0 {suc m} = cong (╬╗ t Рєњ (+ 0) Рѕи t) (vecРёц-replicateTrit0 {m})

zeroVecРёц+рхЦ :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} (v : Vec Рёц m) Рєњ zeroVecРёц {m} +рхЦ v РЅА v
zeroVecРёц+рхЦ {zero} [] = refl
zeroVecРёц+рхЦ {suc m} (x Рѕи xs) =
  congРѓѓ _Рѕи_ (IntP.+-identity╦А x) (zeroVecРёц+рхЦ {m} xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic form on core: sum of squares in Рёц

QcoreРёц : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Рёц
QcoreРёц {m} x =
  let v = vecРёц x in
  sumРёц (map (╬╗ z Рєњ z * z) v)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Correct polarization over the Рёц-embedding:
-- BРѓѓРёц(Q)(x,y) = Q╠ѓ(v(x)+v(y)) - Q╠ѓ(v(x)) - Q╠ѓ(v(y))
-- where Q╠ѓ is a quadratic on Vec Рёц m.

Q╠ѓcore : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Рёц m Рєњ Рёц
Q╠ѓcore v = sumРёц (map (╬╗ z Рєњ z * z) v)

BРѓѓРёц : Рѕђ {m : Nat}
    Рєњ (Q╠ѓ : Vec Рёц m Рєњ Рёц)
    Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Рёц
BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓ x y =
  (Q╠ѓ (vecРёц x +рхЦ vecРёц y)) - (Q╠ѓ (vecРёц x)) - (Q╠ѓ (vecРёц y))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helpers for constructive polarization

-- Scalar polarization identity, specialized to trits.
-- We prove by case split over (neg/zer/pos) ├Ќ (neg/zer/pos);
-- all goals reduce by computation.

b2-trit :
  (a b : Trit) Рєњ
  (intOfTrit a + intOfTrit b) * (intOfTrit a + intOfTrit b)
    - (intOfTrit a * intOfTrit a)
    - (intOfTrit b * intOfTrit b)
    РЅА (+ 2) * (intOfTrit a * intOfTrit b)
b2-trit neg neg = refl
b2-trit neg zer = refl
b2-trit neg pos = refl
b2-trit zer neg = refl
b2-trit zer zer = refl
b2-trit zer pos = refl
b2-trit pos neg = refl
b2-trit pos zer = refl
b2-trit pos pos = refl

postulate
  split-BРѓѓ :
    (A R X RX Y RY : Рёц) Рєњ
    (A + R) - (X + RX) - (Y + RY) РЅА (A - X - Y) + (R - RX - RY)
------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sanity property for Q╠ѓcore (constructive)

Q╠ѓcore-zero :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц (replicateTrit0 m)) РЅА + 0
Q╠ѓcore-zero {zero} = refl
Q╠ѓcore-zero {suc m} =
  cong (╬╗ n Рєњ (+ 0 * + 0) + n) (Q╠ѓcore-zero {m})

BРѓѓРёц-zeroL :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} (x : Vec Trit m) Рєњ
  BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓcore (replicateTrit0 m) x РЅА + 0
BРѓѓРёц-zeroL {m} x =
  begin
    BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓcore (replicateTrit0 m) x
  РЅАРЪе refl РЪЕ
    (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц (replicateTrit0 m) +рхЦ vecРёц x)) - (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц (replicateTrit0 m))) - (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ v Рєњ Q╠ѓcore v - Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц (replicateTrit0 m)) - Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))
        (trans (cong (╬╗ t Рєњ t +рхЦ vecРёц x) (vecРёц-replicateTrit0 {m}))
               (zeroVecРёц+рхЦ (vecРёц x))) РЪЕ
    (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x)) - (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц (replicateTrit0 m))) - (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ z Рєњ Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x) - z - Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))
        (Q╠ѓcore-zero {m}) РЪЕ
    (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x)) - (+ 0) - (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))
  РЅАРЪе refl РЪЕ
    (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x) + (- (+ 0))) + (- Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ t Рєњ Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x) + t + (- Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x)))
        (refl) РЪЕ
    (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x) + (+ 0)) + (- Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ t Рєњ t + (- Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x)))
        (IntP.+-identity╩│ (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))) РЪЕ
    (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x)) + (- Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x))
  РЅАРЪе IntP.+-inverse╩│ (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц x)) РЪЕ
    + 0
  Рѕј

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Main target theorem to chase:
-- For Q╠ѓcore(v)=РѕЉ vрхб┬▓ we should have:
--   BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓcore x y = 2 * dotРёц (vecРёц x) (vecРёц y)

BРѓѓРёц-Q╠ѓcore-dot2 :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit m) Рєњ
  BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓcore x y РЅА ((+ 2) * dotРёц (vecРёц x) (vecРёц y))
BРѓѓРёц-Q╠ѓcore-dot2 [] [] =
  begin
    BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓcore [] []
  РЅАРЪе refl РЪЕ
    + 0
  РЅАРЪе sym (IntP.*-zero╩│ (+ 2)) РЪЕ
    (+ 2) * (+ 0)
  Рѕј
BРѓѓРёц-Q╠ѓcore-dot2 (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys) =
  begin
    BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓcore (x Рѕи xs) (y Рѕи ys)
  РЅАРЪе refl РЪЕ
    (Q╠ѓcore ((vecРёц (x Рѕи xs)) +рхЦ (vecРёц (y Рѕи ys))))
      - (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц (x Рѕи xs)))
      - (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц (y Рѕи ys)))
  РЅАРЪе refl РЪЕ
    ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y)
      + Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц xs +рхЦ vecРёц ys))
      - ((intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x) + Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц xs))
      - ((intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y) + Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц ys))
  РЅАРЪе split-BРѓѓ
        ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y))
        (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц xs +рхЦ vecРёц ys))
        (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x)
        (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц xs))
        (intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y)
        (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц ys)) РЪЕ
    ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y)
      - (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x)
      - (intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y))
      + (Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц xs +рхЦ vecРёц ys) - Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц xs) - Q╠ѓcore (vecРёц ys))
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ t Рєњ t + (BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓcore xs ys)) (b2-trit x y) РЪЕ
    ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + (BРѓѓРёц Q╠ѓcore xs ys)
  РЅАРЪе cong (╬╗ t Рєњ ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + t) (BРѓѓРёц-Q╠ѓcore-dot2 xs ys) РЪЕ
    ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + ((+ 2) * dotРёц (vecРёц xs) (vecРёц ys))
  РЅАРЪе sym (IntP.*-distrib╦А-+ (+ 2) (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y) (dotРёц (vecРёц xs) (vecРёц ys))) РЪЕ
    (+ 2) * ((intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y) + dotРёц (vecРёц xs) (vecРёц ys))
  Рѕј
  where
    open Рёц-Reasoning

module DASHI.Physics.SignatureClassificationBridge where

  field
    p : Nat
    q : Nat

  (T : S Рєњ S)
  : SetРѓЂ where
  field

    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U T

      Рѕђ {S : Set} {U : UMetric.Ultrametric S} {T : S Рєњ S} Рєњ
      (out : CQ.QuadraticOutput) Рєњ

  sig : Signature
  sig = classify qs (CQ.out cq) sym
module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseMetricProof where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (╬Б; _,_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; replicate)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail collapse implies distance-to-neutral is zero

tailCollapse-distance0 :
  Рѕђ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.iterate k TCP.tailStep t) (replicate k zer) РЅА 0
tailCollapse-distance0 k t =
  let
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit k)
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = k}

    open UMetric.Ultrametric U using (id-zero)
  in
  trans
    (cong (╬╗ x Рєњ FAM.dNatFine x (replicate k zer)) (TCP.tailCollapse k t))
    (id-zero (replicate k zer))

tailCollapse-finiteTime :
  Рѕђ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  ╬Б Nat (╬╗ N Рєњ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.iterate N TCP.tailStep t) (replicate k zer) РЅА 0)
tailCollapse-finiteTime k t = (k , tailCollapse-distance0 k t)

tailCollapse-fullState-distance0 :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TрхБ {m} {k}) x)) (replicate k zer) РЅА 0
tailCollapse-fullState-distance0 m k x =
  let
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit k)
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = k}

    open UMetric.Ultrametric U using (id-zero)
  in
  trans
    (cong (╬╗ y Рєњ FAM.dNatFine y (replicate k zer)) (TCP.tailOf-after-Tk m k x))
    (id-zero (replicate k zer))
module DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans; substРѓѓ)

open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_; projРѓЂ; projРѓѓ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; _++_; map)

open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Minimal nontrivial canonicalization on a single Trit

canonTrit : Trit Рєњ Trit
canonTrit neg = pos
canonTrit zer = zer
canonTrit pos = pos

canonVec : Рѕђ {n : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit n Рєњ Vec Trit n
canonVec = map canonTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization on the full state: act only on the coarse core

CрхБ : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k) Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k)
CрхБ {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) = canonVec c ++ t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansiveness (constructive)

CрхБ-++ :
  Рѕђ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  CрхБ {m} {k} (c ++ t) РЅА canonVec c ++ t
CрхБ-++ {m} {k} c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t = refl

nonexpCрхБ :
  Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ
  SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (CрхБ {m} {k})
nonexpCрхБ {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : Рѕђ x y Рєњ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (CрхБ {m} {k} x) (CрхБ {m} {k} y)
                       РЅц UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        p : x РЅА TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y РЅА TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : CрхБ {m} {k} x РЅА canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k x) ++ TCP.tailOf m k x
        r = trans (cong (╬╗ v Рєњ CрхБ {m} {k} v) p)
                  (CрхБ-++ (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.tailOf m k x))
        s : CрхБ {m} {k} y РЅА canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k y) ++ TCP.tailOf m k y
        s = trans (cong (╬╗ v Рєњ CрхБ {m} {k} v) q)
                  (CрхБ-++ (TCP.coarseOf m k y) (TCP.tailOf m k y))
        lhs : FAM.dNatFine (canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k x) ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                            (canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k y) ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
              РЅц FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                             (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
        lhs = FAM.dNatFine-++-mapРЅц
                (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.coarseOf m k y)
                (TCP.tailOf m k x) (TCP.tailOf m k y)
                canonTrit
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (CрхБ {m} {k} x) (CрхБ {m} {k} y)
                РЅц FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                               (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
        step1 =
          substРѓѓ
            (╬╗ a b Рєњ FAM.dNatFine a b РЅц FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                                                     (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y))
            (sym r) (sym s) lhs
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                             (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
                             РЅА FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 =
          substРѓѓ
            (╬╗ x' y' Рєњ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                                   (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
                                   РЅА FAM.dNatFine x' y')
            (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.РЅц-trans step1 (NatP.РЅц-reflexive step2)
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedConeStructure where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Data.Empty using (РіЦ)
open import Data.Integer using (Рёц; +_) renaming (_РЅц_ to _РЅцрхб_; _<_ to _<рхб_)
open import Data.Nat renaming (_РЅц_ to _РЅцРѓЎ_) hiding (_<_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.SignatureFromMask as SFM

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone predicates

Timelike : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec IMQ.Sign m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Set
Timelike ¤Ѓ x = (+ 0) <рхб IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x

Spacelike : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec IMQ.Sign m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Set
Spacelike ¤Ѓ x = IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x <рхб (+ 0)

Null : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec IMQ.Sign m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Set
Null ¤Ѓ x = IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ x РЅА (+ 0)

    _РЅ╝_  : Vec Trit m Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Set

-- if x РЅ╝ y then Q¤Ѓ(delta x y) РЅЦ 0

postulate
  coneMonotone :
    Рѕђ {m : Nat} (¤Ѓ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (C : CausalStructure m) (x y : Vec Trit m) Рєњ
    CausalStructure._РЅ╝_ C x y Рєњ
    (+ 0) РЅцрхб IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ (CausalStructure.delta C x y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

TwoTimeLike : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec IMQ.Sign m Рєњ Set
TwoTimeLike ¤Ѓ = (suc (suc 0)) РЅцРѓЎ SFM.countMinus ¤Ѓ

record UniqueFixedPoint {A : Set} (T : A Рєњ A) : Set where

    fp : A

module DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

C : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ RTC.Carrier (m + k) Рєњ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
C {m} {k} = CM.CрхБ {m} {k}

P : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ RTC.Carrier (m + k) Рєњ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
P {m} {k} = TCP.PрхБ {m} {k}

R : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ RTC.Carrier (m + k) Рєњ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
R {m} {k} = TCP.RрхБ {m} {k}

nonexpC : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (C {m} {k})
nonexpC {m} {k} = CM.nonexpCрхБ {m} {k}

nonexpR : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (R {m} {k})
nonexpR {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : Рѕђ x y Рєњ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (R {m} {k} x) (R {m} {k} y)
                       РЅц UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        cx = TCP.coarseOf m k x
        tx = TCP.tailOf m k x
        cy = TCP.coarseOf m k y
        ty = TCP.tailOf m k y
        p : x РЅА cx ++ tx
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y РЅА cy ++ ty
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : R {m} {k} x РЅА cx ++ TCP.shiftTail tx
        r = trans (cong (╬╗ v Рєњ R {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.RрхБ-++ m k cx tx)
        s : R {m} {k} y РЅА cy ++ TCP.shiftTail ty
        s = trans (cong (╬╗ v Рєњ R {m} {k} v) q) (TCP.RрхБ-++ m k cy ty)
        step : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ TCP.shiftTail tx) (cy ++ TCP.shiftTail ty)
               РЅц FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step = FAM.dNatFine-++-shiftTailРЅц cx cy tx ty
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (R {m} {k} x) (R {m} {k} y)
                 РЅц FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step1 =
          substРѓѓ
            (╬╗ a b Рєњ FAM.dNatFine a b РЅц FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty))
            (sym r) (sym s) step
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) РЅА FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 = substРѓѓ
          (╬╗ x' y' Рєњ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) РЅА FAM.dNatFine x' y')
          (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.РЅц-trans step1 (NatP.РЅц-reflexive step2)

nonexpP : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k})
nonexpP {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : Рѕђ x y Рєњ
      UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y)
        РЅц UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        cx = TCP.coarseOf m k x
        tx = TCP.tailOf m k x
        cy = TCP.coarseOf m k y
        ty = TCP.tailOf m k y
        p : x РЅА cx ++ tx
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y РЅА cy ++ ty
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : P {m} {k} x РЅА cx ++ TCP.projTail tx
        r = trans (cong (╬╗ v Рєњ P {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.PрхБ-++ m k cx tx)
        s : P {m} {k} y РЅА cy ++ TCP.projTail ty
        s = trans (cong (╬╗ v Рєњ P {m} {k} v) q) (TCP.PрхБ-++ m k cy ty)
        step : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ TCP.projTail tx) (cy ++ TCP.projTail ty)
               РЅц FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step = FAM.dNatFine-++-projTailРЅц cx cy tx ty
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y)
                 РЅц FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step1 =
          substРѓѓ
            (╬╗ a b Рєњ FAM.dNatFine a b РЅц FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty))
            (sym r) (sym s) step
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) РЅА FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 = substРѓѓ
          (╬╗ x' y' Рєњ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) РЅА FAM.dNatFine x' y')
          (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.РЅц-trans step1 (NatP.РЅц-reflexive step2)

strictP-fiber :
  Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ
  FC.ContractiveOnFibers (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k})
strictP-fiber {m} {k} =
  record
    { contractFiber = ╬╗ {x} {y} fd Рєњ
        let
          open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
          open FC.FiberDistinct fd using (xРЅбy; sameFiber)
          d0 : d (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y) РЅА 0
          d0 = subst (╬╗ z Рєњ d (P {m} {k} x) z РЅА 0) sameFiber (id-zero (P {m} {k} x))
        in
        subst (╬╗ u Рєњ u < d x y) (sym d0) (FAM.dNatFine-positive xРЅбy)
    }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticCore where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym)
