------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic РђюenergyРђЮ density per trit: squares of {-1,0,+1}
-- Encoded directly as Nat: 1 for ┬▒, 0 for 0.

sqTrit : Trit Рєњ Nat
sqTrit neg = 1
sqTrit zer = 0
sqTrit pos = 1

sumNat : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Nat m Рєњ Nat
sumNat [] = 0
sumNat (x Рѕи xs) = x + sumNat xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic invariant on the core: sum of squares

Qcore : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Nat
Qcore c = sumNat (map sqTrit c)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization preserves squares pointwise

sq-canon : Рѕђ t Рєњ sqTrit (CM.canonTrit t) РЅА sqTrit t
sq-canon neg = refl
sq-canon zer = refl
sq-canon pos = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Qcore invariance under canonVec

Qcore-canonVec : Рѕђ {m : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) Рєњ Qcore (CM.canonVec c) РЅА Qcore c
Qcore-canonVec [] = refl
Qcore-canonVec (t Рѕи ts)
  rewrite sq-canon t
  = cong (╬╗ n Рєњ sqTrit t + n) (Qcore-canonVec ts)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift Qcore to the full state via the coarse split

Qfull : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k) Рєњ Nat
Qfull {m} {k} x = Qcore (TCP.coarseOf m k x)

Qfull-invariant-CрхБ :
  Рѕђ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  Qfull {m} {k} (CM.CрхБ {m} {k} x) РЅА Qfull {m} {k} x
Qfull-invariant-CрхБ {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | p
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k (CM.canonVec (projРѓЂ p)) (projРѓѓ p)
        | TCP.split-++ m k (projРѓЂ p) (projРѓѓ p)
  = Qcore-canonVec (projРѓЂ p)

module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_; projРѓЂ; projРѓѓ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_; _++_; replicate)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (take; init; last; _Рѕи╩│_)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete, nontrivial renormalization RрхБ implementing a Рђюscale shiftРђЮ
------------------------------------------------------------------------

split :
  Рѕђ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) Рєњ
  Vec A (m + k) Рєњ (Vec A m ├Ќ Vec A k)
split {A} zero    k xs       = ([] , xs)
split {A} (suc m) k (x Рѕи xs) with split {A} m k xs
... | (c , t) = (x Рѕи c , t)

split-++ :
  Рѕђ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) (c : Vec A m) (t : Vec A k) Рєњ
  split m k (c ++ t) РЅА (c , t)
split-++ zero k [] t = refl
split-++ (suc m) k (x Рѕи xs) t =
  cong (╬╗ p Рєњ (x Рѕи projРѓЂ p , projРѓѓ p)) (split-++ m k xs t)

coarseOf : Рѕђ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) Рєњ Vec A (m + k) Рєњ Vec A m
coarseOf m k x = projРѓЂ (split m k x)

tailOf : Рѕђ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) Рєњ Vec A (m + k) Рєњ Vec A k
tailOf m k x = projРѓѓ (split m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail-band operators

shiftTail : Рѕђ {k : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit k Рєњ Vec Trit k
shiftTail {zero}    []       = []
shiftTail {suc kРђ▓}  (x Рѕи xs) = xs Рѕи╩│ zer

projTail : Рѕђ {k : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit k Рєњ Vec Trit k
projTail {zero}    []       = []
projTail {suc kРђ▓}  t        = (init t) Рѕи╩│ zer

tailStep : Рѕђ {k : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit k Рєњ Vec Trit k
tailStep t = projTail (shiftTail t)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift tail-band operators to full state

RрхБ : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k) Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k)
RрхБ {m} {k} x with split m k x
... | (c , t) = c ++ shiftTail t

PрхБ : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k) Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k)
PрхБ {m} {k} x with split m k x
... | (c , t) = c ++ projTail t

RрхБ-++ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  RрхБ {m} {k} (c ++ t) РЅА c ++ shiftTail t
RрхБ-++ m k c t rewrite split-++ m k c t = refl

PрхБ-++ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  PрхБ {m} {k} (c ++ t) РЅА c ++ projTail t
PрхБ-++ m k c t rewrite split-++ m k c t = refl

TрхБ : Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k) Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k)
TрхБ {m} {k} x = PрхБ {m} {k} (RрхБ {m} {k} x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration

iterate : Рѕђ {A : Set} Рєњ Nat Рєњ (A Рєњ A) Рєњ A Рєњ A
iterate zero    f x = x
iterate (suc n) f x = iterate n f (f x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time tail collapse

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helper lemmas for replicate

init-replicate :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} Рєњ init (replicate (suc k) zer) РЅА replicate k zer
init-replicate {zero} = refl
init-replicate {suc k} =
  cong (╬╗ t Рєњ zer Рѕи t) (init-replicate {k})

snoc-replicate :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} Рєњ (replicate k zer) Рѕи╩│ zer РЅА replicate (suc k) zer
snoc-replicate {zero} = refl
snoc-replicate {suc k} =
  cong (╬╗ t Рєњ zer Рѕи t) (snoc-replicate {k})

tailStep-forgets-last :
  Рѕђ {kРђ▓ : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc kРђ▓)) Рєњ
  tailStep t РЅА projTail (shiftTail t)
tailStep-forgets-last {kРђ▓} t = refl

projTail-replicate :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} Рєњ projTail (replicate k zer) РЅА replicate k zer
projTail-replicate {zero}    = refl
projTail-replicate {suc kРђ▓}  =
  trans
    (cong (_Рѕи╩│ zer) (init-replicate {kРђ▓}))
    (snoc-replicate {kРђ▓})

shiftTail-replicate :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} Рєњ shiftTail (replicate k zer) РЅА replicate k zer
shiftTail-replicate {zero}   = refl
shiftTail-replicate {suc kРђ▓} =
  snoc-replicate {kРђ▓}

tailStep-replicate :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} Рєњ tailStep (replicate k zer) РЅА replicate k zer
tailStep-replicate {k} =
  trans (cong projTail (shiftTail-replicate {k}))
        (projTail-replicate {k})

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Extra Vec lemmas needed for constructive nilpotence
------------------------------------------------------------------------

pair-╬и : Рѕђ {A B : Set} (p : A ├Ќ B) Рєњ (projРѓЂ p , projРѓѓ p) РЅА p
pair-╬и (a , b) = refl

init-Рѕи╩│ : Рѕђ {A : Set} {n : Nat} (xs : Vec A n) (a : A) Рєњ init (xs Рѕи╩│ a) РЅА xs
init-Рѕи╩│ {n = zero}    []       a = refl
init-Рѕи╩│ {n = suc n} (x Рѕи xs) a rewrite init-Рѕи╩│ xs a = refl

tailStepРЅАshiftTail : Рѕђ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ tailStep t РЅА shiftTail t
tailStepРЅАshiftTail {zero}    [] = refl
tailStepРЅАshiftTail {suc kРђ▓} (x Рѕи xs)
  rewrite init-Рѕи╩│ xs zer
  = refl

shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  shiftTail (xs Рѕи╩│ zer) РЅА (shiftTail xs) Рѕи╩│ zer
shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer {zero} [] = refl
shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer {suc k} (x Рѕи xs) = refl

iterate-shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer :
  Рѕђ {k : Nat} (n : Nat) (xs : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  iterate n shiftTail (xs Рѕи╩│ zer) РЅА (iterate n shiftTail xs) Рѕи╩│ zer
iterate-shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer zero xs = refl
iterate-shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer (suc n) xs
  rewrite shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer xs
        | iterate-shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer n (shiftTail xs)
  = refl

iterate-pointwise :
  Рѕђ {A : Set} (n : Nat) (f g : A Рєњ A) (x : A) Рєњ
  (Рѕђ y Рєњ f y РЅА g y) Рєњ
  iterate n f x РЅА iterate n g x
iterate-pointwise zero f g x fg = refl
iterate-pointwise (suc n) f g x fg
  rewrite fg x
  = iterate-pointwise n f g (g x) fg

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time tail collapse (constructive)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

tailCollapse-shiftTail :
  Рѕђ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  iterate k shiftTail t РЅА replicate k zer
tailCollapse-shiftTail zero    []       = refl
tailCollapse-shiftTail (suc k) (x Рѕи xs) =
  trans
    (iterate-shiftTail-Рѕи╩│-zer k xs)
    (trans
      (cong (_Рѕи╩│ zer) (tailCollapse-shiftTail k xs))
      (snoc-replicate {k}))

tailCollapse :
  Рѕђ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  iterate k tailStep t РЅА replicate k zer
tailCollapse k t =
  trans
    (iterate-pointwise k tailStep shiftTail t (╬╗ y Рєњ tailStepРЅАshiftTail y))
    (tailCollapse-shiftTail k t)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lifted corollary: full state tail band collapses in k steps

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lifted corollary: full state tail band collapses in k steps (constructive)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

merge-split :
  Рѕђ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) (x : Vec A (m + k)) Рєњ
  (coarseOf m k x ++ tailOf m k x) РЅА x
merge-split {A} zero    k x = refl
merge-split {A} (suc m) k (x Рѕи xs)
  rewrite merge-split {A} m k xs
  = refl

TрхБ-++ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  TрхБ {m} {k} (c ++ t) РЅА c ++ tailStep t
TрхБ-++ m k c t
  rewrite RрхБ-++ m k c t
        | PрхБ-++ m k c (shiftTail t)
  = refl

split-TрхБ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  split m k (TрхБ {m} {k} x) РЅА (coarseOf m k x , tailStep (tailOf m k x))
split-TрхБ m k x with split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite RрхБ-++ m k c t
        | PрхБ-++ m k c (shiftTail t)
        | split-++ m k c (projTail (shiftTail t))
  = refl

split-iterate-TрхБ :
  Рѕђ (m k n : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  split m k (iterate n (TрхБ {m} {k}) x) РЅА
    ( coarseOf m k x
    , iterate n tailStep (tailOf m k x)
    )
split-iterate-TрхБ m k zero x
  = sym (pair-╬и (split m k x))
split-iterate-TрхБ m k (suc n) x
  rewrite split-iterate-TрхБ m k n (TрхБ {m} {k} x)
        | split-TрхБ m k x
  = refl

tailOf-after-Tk :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  tailOf m k (iterate k (TрхБ {m} {k}) x) РЅА replicate k zer
tailOf-after-Tk m k x =
  trans
    (cong projРѓѓ (split-iterate-TрхБ m k k x))
    (tailCollapse k (tailOf m k x))

invVec {n} = map inv

invVec-invol : Рѕђ {n} (x : Carrier n) Рєњ invVec (invVec x) РЅА x
invVec-invol [] = refl
invVec-invol (t Рѕи ts) rewrite inv-invol t | invVec-invol ts = refl

zeroVec : Рѕђ {n} Рєњ Carrier n
zeroVec {n = zero} = []
zeroVec {n = suc n} = zer Рѕи zeroVec {n}

module DASHI.Physics.DefaultClosure where

open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat using (_РЅц_; _<_; _Ріћ_; zРЅцn; sРЅцs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete, total instance to close the physics glue
------------------------------------------------------------------------

_РЅб_ : Рѕђ {A : Set} Рєњ A Рєњ A Рєњ Set
x РЅб y = x РЅА y Рєњ РіЦ

Carrier : Set
Carrier = Bool

-- Discrete ultrametric on Bool: 0 if equal, 1 otherwise.
dBool : Carrier Рєњ Carrier Рєњ Nat
dBool true  true  = zero
dBool false false = zero
dBool true  false = suc zero
dBool false true  = suc zero

id-zeroBool : Рѕђ x Рєњ dBool x x РЅА 0
id-zeroBool true  = refl
id-zeroBool false = refl

symBool : Рѕђ x y Рєњ dBool x y РЅА dBool y x
symBool true  true  = refl
symBool false false = refl
symBool true  false = refl
symBool false true  = refl

ultratriangleBool : Рѕђ x y z Рєњ dBool x z РЅц (dBool x y Ріћ dBool y z)
ultratriangleBool true  true  true  = zРЅцn
ultratriangleBool true  true  false = sРЅцs zРЅцn
ultratriangleBool true  false true  = zРЅцn
ultratriangleBool true  false false = sРЅцs zРЅцn
ultratriangleBool false true  true  = sРЅцs zРЅцn
ultratriangleBool false true  false = zРЅцn
ultratriangleBool false false true  = sРЅцs zРЅцn
ultratriangleBool false false false = zРЅцn

boolUltrametric : UMetric.Ultrametric Carrier
boolUltrametric =
  record
    { d = dBool
    ; id-zero = id-zeroBool
    ; symmetric = symBool
    ; ultratriangle = ultratriangleBool
    }

-- Constant contraction to false.
T : Carrier Рєњ Carrier
T _ = false

contractiveBool-proof : Рѕђ x y Рєњ x РЅб y Рєњ dBool (T x) (T y) < dBool x y
contractiveBool-proof true  false _   = sРЅцs zРЅцn
contractiveBool-proof false true  _   = sРЅцs zРЅцn
contractiveBool-proof true  true  xРЅбy = РіЦ-elim (xРЅбy refl)
contractiveBool-proof false false xРЅбy = РіЦ-elim (xРЅбy refl)

contractiveBool : Contraction.ContractiveРЅб boolUltrametric T
contractiveBool =
  record
    { contractionРЅб = ╬╗ {x} {y} xРЅбy Рєњ
        contractiveBool-proof x y xРЅбy
    }

boolTrueNeqFalse : false РЅА true Рєњ РіЦ
boolTrueNeqFalse ()

uniqueBool : Рѕђ x Рєњ T x РЅА x Рєњ x РЅА false
uniqueBool true  hx = РіЦ-elim (boolTrueNeqFalse hx)
uniqueBool false _  = refl

strictBool : Contraction.StrictContraction boolUltrametric T
strictBool =
  record
    { contractiveРЅб = contractiveBool
    ; fp = false
    ; fixed = refl
    ; unique = uniqueBool
    }

invBool : Involution Carrier
invBool = record
  { ╬╣ = ╬╗ x Рєњ x
  ; invol = ╬╗ _ Рєњ refl
  }

defaultClosure : Glue.ClosureAxioms
defaultClosure = Glue.mkDefaultClosure boolUltrametric T strictBool invBool

defaultClosureStatus : ClosureStatus
defaultClosureStatus = closureStatusFromGlue defaultClosure

module DASHI.Physics.SignatureFromMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; congРѓѓ)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _Рѕи_)
open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_)

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic using (Sign; plus; minus)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Count plus/minus in a mask and extract signature

countPlus : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Sign m Рєњ Nat
countPlus [] = 0
countPlus (plus  Рѕи ¤Ѓ) = suc (countPlus ¤Ѓ)
countPlus (minus Рѕи ¤Ѓ) = countPlus ¤Ѓ

countMinus : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Sign m Рєњ Nat
countMinus [] = 0
countMinus (plus  Рѕи ¤Ѓ) = countMinus ¤Ѓ
countMinus (minus Рѕи ¤Ѓ) = suc (countMinus ¤Ѓ)

signature : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Sign m Рєњ Nat ├Ќ Nat
signature ¤Ѓ = (countMinus ¤Ѓ , countPlus ¤Ѓ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete mask constructor: one minus, rest plus

replicatePlus : Рѕђ (k : Nat) Рєњ Vec Sign k
replicatePlus zero    = []
replicatePlus (suc k) = plus Рѕи replicatePlus k

oneMinusRestPlus : Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ Vec Sign (suc m)
oneMinusRestPlus {m} = minus Рѕи replicatePlus m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Signature of the concrete mask

countPlus-replicatePlus :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ countPlus (replicatePlus m) РЅА m
countPlus-replicatePlus {zero} = refl
countPlus-replicatePlus {suc m} =
  cong suc (countPlus-replicatePlus {m})

countMinus-replicatePlus :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ countMinus (replicatePlus m) РЅА 0
countMinus-replicatePlus {zero} = refl
countMinus-replicatePlus {suc m} = countMinus-replicatePlus {m}

signature-oneMinus :
  Рѕђ {m : Nat} Рєњ signature (oneMinusRestPlus {m}) РЅА (suc 0 , m)
signature-oneMinus {m} =
  congРѓѓ _,_
    (cong suc (countMinus-replicatePlus {m}))
    (countPlus-replicatePlus {m})

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedQuadraticRenormalization where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_; projРѓЂ; projРѓѓ)
open import Data.Integer using (Рёц; _*_) renaming (_+_ to _+Рёц_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedSplitQuadratic as MSQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic split lemmas for coarse/tail under concatenation

coarseOf-++ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  TCP.coarseOf m k (c ++ t) РЅА c
coarseOf-++ m k c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t
  = refl

tailOf-++ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  TCP.tailOf m k (c ++ t) РЅА t
tailOf-++ m k c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Coarse/tail behavior under renormalization RрхБ

coarseOf-RрхБ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.RрхБ {m} {k} x) РЅА TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarseOf-RрхБ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RрхБ-++ m k c t
        | coarseOf-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

tailOf-RрхБ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.RрхБ {m} {k} x) РЅА TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-RрхБ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RрхБ-++ m k c t
        | tailOf-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

RрхБ-decomp :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  TCP.RрхБ {m} {k} x РЅА TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
RрхБ-decomp m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RрхБ-++ m k c t
        | coarseOf-++ m k c t
        | tailOf-++ m k c t
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic under renormalization:
-- Q¤Ѓ(RрхБ x) splits into coarse + shifted tail.

Q¤Ѓ-split-++ :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat)
    (¤Ѓc : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (¤Ѓt : Vec IMQ.Sign k)
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  IMQ.Q¤Ѓ (¤Ѓc ++ ¤Ѓt) (c ++ t)
    РЅА IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓc c +Рёц IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓt t
Q¤Ѓ-split-++ m k ¤Ѓc ¤Ѓt c t =
  let
    f = (╬╗ s xi Рєњ IMQ.signРёц s * IMQ.sqРёц (IMQ.toРёцTrit xi))
  in
  trans
    refl
    (trans
      (cong IMQ.sumРёц (MSQ.zipWith-++ f ¤Ѓc ¤Ѓt c t))
      (trans
        (MSQ.sumРёц-++ (zipWith f ¤Ѓc c) (zipWith f ¤Ѓt t))
        refl))

Q¤Ѓ-split-coarse :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat)
    (¤Ѓ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) Рєњ
  IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ (c ++ t)
    РЅА IMQ.Q¤Ѓ (TCP.coarseOf m k ¤Ѓ) c
    +Рёц IMQ.Q¤Ѓ (TCP.tailOf m k ¤Ѓ) t
Q¤Ѓ-split-coarse m k ¤Ѓ c t
  =
  trans
    (cong (╬╗ z Рєњ IMQ.Q¤Ѓ z (c ++ t)) (sym (TCP.merge-split {A = IMQ.Sign} m k ¤Ѓ)))
    (Q¤Ѓ-split-++ m k (TCP.coarseOf m k ¤Ѓ) (TCP.tailOf m k ¤Ѓ) c t)

Q¤Ѓ-R :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat)
    (¤Ѓ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  IMQ.Q¤Ѓ ¤Ѓ (TCP.RрхБ {m} {k} x)
    РЅА IMQ.Q¤Ѓ (TCP.coarseOf m k ¤Ѓ) (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    +Рёц IMQ.Q¤Ѓ (TCP.tailOf   m k ¤Ѓ) (TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x))
Q¤Ѓ-R m k ¤Ѓ x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RрхБ-++ m k c t
  = Q¤Ѓ-split-coarse m k ¤Ѓ c (TCP.shiftTail t)
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedClosureKit where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Integer using (Рёц)

open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic invariants wired onto a RealClosureKitFiber instance.
--
-- This does not change the underlying closure kit; it augments it with:
--   - a mask on the core,
--   - the masked quadratic Q¤Ѓ and bilinear BРѓѓ¤Ѓ pulled back to the full state,
--   - a signature extracted from the mask,
--   - an orbit-profile seam (dimension bound target).

record RealClosureKitFiberMask : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    m k : Nat
    base : RKF.RealClosureKitFiber

    -- Mask on the core (length m).
    mask : Vec IMQ.Sign m

    -- Core-only invariants, lifted to the full state via coarseOf.
    coreQ¤Ѓ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) Рєњ Рёц
    coreB2¤Ѓ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) Рєњ RTC.Carrier (m + k) Рєњ Рёц

    -- Signature extracted from the mask.
    sig : Nat ├Ќ Nat

    -- Orbit-profile seam (dimension-bound target).
    orbitProfile : DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m

open RealClosureKitFiberMask public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Constructor: derive all fields from base + mask.

mkMaskKit :
  Рѕђ {m k : Nat} Рєњ
  RKF.RealClosureKitFiber Рєњ
  Vec IMQ.Sign m Рєњ
  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m Рєњ
  RealClosureKitFiberMask
mkMaskKit {m} {k} base mask orbitProfile =
  record
    { m = m
    ; k = k
    ; base = base
    ; mask = mask
    ; coreQ¤Ѓ = ╬╗ x Рєњ IMQ.Q¤Ѓ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    ; coreB2¤Ѓ = ╬╗ x y Рєњ IMQ.B2¤Ѓ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.coarseOf m k y)
    ; sig = SFM.signature mask
    ; orbitProfile = orbitProfile
    }

module DASHI.Physics.LiftToFullState where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_├Ќ_; _,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; replicate)

open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Invariant coarse subspace

embedCoarse : Рѕђ (m k : Nat) Рєњ Vec Trit m Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k)
embedCoarse m k c = c ++ replicate k zer

coarseProj : Рѕђ (m k : Nat) Рєњ Vec Trit (m + k) Рєњ Vec Trit m
coarseProj m k x = TCP.coarseOf m k x

coarse-invariant-R :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  coarseProj m k (TCP.RрхБ {m} {k} x) РЅА coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-R m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t) = refl

coarse-invariant-P :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  coarseProj m k (TCP.PрхБ {m} {k} x) РЅА coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-P m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t) = refl

coarse-invariant-T :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  coarseProj m k (TCP.TрхБ {m} {k} x) РЅА coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-T m k x =
  trans (coarse-invariant-P m k (TCP.RрхБ {m} {k} x))
        (coarse-invariant-R m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time collapse + invariant geometry, packaged

coarse-invariant-iter :
  Рѕђ (m k n : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  coarseProj m k (TCP.iterate n (TCP.TрхБ {m} {k}) x) РЅА coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-iter m k zero x = refl
coarse-invariant-iter m k (suc n) x =
  trans
    (coarse-invariant-iter m k n (TCP.TрхБ {m} {k} x))
    (coarse-invariant-T m k x)

finiteTimeCollapse-to-geometry :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) Рєњ
  ( coarseProj m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TрхБ {m} {k}) x) РЅА coarseProj m k x )
  ├Ќ
  ( TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TрхБ {m} {k}) x) РЅА replicate k zer )
finiteTimeCollapse-to-geometry m k x =
  ( coarse-invariant-iter m k k x
  , TCP.tailOf-after-Tk m k x
  )

invariantCoarseSubspace :
  Рѕђ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) Рєњ
  TCP.TрхБ {m} {k} (embedCoarse m k c) РЅА embedCoarse m k c
invariantCoarseSubspace m k c
  rewrite TCP.RрхБ-++ m k c (replicate k zer)
        | TCP.PрхБ-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail (replicate k zer))
        | TCP.shiftTail-replicate {k}
        | TCP.projTail-replicate {k}
  = refl

module Verification.Prelude where

  renaming (РёЋ to Nat)

┬г_ : Set Рєњ Set
┬г A = A Рєњ РіЦ

fst : {A : Set} {B : A Рєњ Set} Рєњ ╬Б A B Рєњ A
fst = projРѓЂ

module Verification.ZK where

open import Verification.Prelude

postulate Public  : Set
postulate Private : Set
postulate Output  : Set

-- The spec function (what correctness means)
postulate spec : Public -> Private -> Output

-- An implementation whose correctness you want to prove (could be a circuit)
postulate impl : Public -> Private -> Output

-- A proof object (SNARK) and a verifier predicate
postulate Proof : Set
postulate verify : Public -> Output -> Proof -> Bool

-- Soundness contract (non-ZK): if verifier accepts, output equals spec
-- (This is where you plug the cryptographic theorem/certificate.)
postulate
  zkSoundness :
    (pub : Public) -> (priv : Private) -> (out : Output) -> (pi : Proof) ->
    verify pub out pi РЅА true ->
    out РЅА spec pub priv

-- ZK verification artifact: provide pub/out/proof and a verification boolean proof.
record ZKCorrectness : Set1 where
  field
    pub  : Public
    priv : Private
    out  : Output
    pi   : Proof
    accepts : verify pub out pi РЅА true
    correct : out РЅА spec pub priv
module Verification.ExecutionReview where

open import Verification.Prelude

-- A tiny abstract control-flow model.
postulate Program : Set
postulate Path    : Set

-- Static analyzer produces a set/list of feasible paths
postulate enumeratePaths : Program Рєњ List Path

-- A property you claim holds on all paths.
postulate SafeOnPath : Program Рєњ Path Рєњ Set

-- РђюExecution reviewРђЮ = proof that for every enumerated path, Safe holds.
All : Рѕђ {A : Set} Рєњ (A Рєњ Set) Рєњ List A Рєњ Set
All P []       = Ріц
All P (x Рѕи xs) = P x ├Ќ All P xs

record ExecutionReview : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    P   : Program
    ok  : All (SafeOnPath P) (enumeratePaths P)
module Verification.SourceHash where

open import Verification.Prelude

-- Abstract bytes; you can refine to Word8 later.

Bytes = List Byte

-- Cryptographic hash as a function (model-level).
postulate Hash : Set

-- A repo snapshot is modeled as its bytes (tarball) + declared hash.
record Snapshot : Set where
  constructor snap
  field
    blob     : Bytes
    declared : Hash

-- Integrity proof obligation: declared equals computed.
record SourceIntegrity : Set where
  field
    S : Snapshot
    ok : Snapshot.declared S РЅА hash (Snapshot.blob S)
module Verification.BinaryPatching where

postulate Binary : Set

postulate Output : Set

    -- behavior preserved on some agreed safe domain
    preserved : Рѕђ i Рєњ SafeInput i Рєњ run (patch B) i РЅА run B i

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distance function into РёЋ (discrete ultrametric)

record Ultrametric (S : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    d : S Рєњ S Рєњ Nat

    -- Identity
    id-zero :
      Рѕђ x Рєњ d x x РЅА 0

    -- Symmetry
    symmetric :
      Рѕђ x y Рєњ d x y РЅА d y x

    -- Strong triangle inequality (ultrametric)
    ultratriangle :
      Рѕђ x y z Рєњ
      d x z РЅц max (d x y) (d y z)

module CRTPeriod where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_)

open import Data.Nat.Base   using (nonZero)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (_%_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Repo-defined digit function:

d : Nat Рєњ Nat
d N = ((N % 71) + (N % 59) + (N % 47)) % 10

period : Nat
period = 71 * 59 * 47  -- 196883

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The theorem statement (R1):
-- d(N + k*period) = d(N) for all k.
--
-- Proof is standard modular arithmetic:
-- (N + k*period) mod p = N mod p for p Рѕѕ {71,59,47}
-- then propagate through sum and mod 10.
--
-- You can discharge this using stdlib DivMod lemmas, or (DASHI-style)
-- by importing a small proof certificate.

postulate
  period-thm : Рѕђ N k Рєњ d (N + k * period) РЅА d N
module Z6_RegularInverse where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Z6 elements as Fin 6

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ring operations modulo 6 (postulate or implement via Fin arithmetic).
-- If you want full concreteness, implement add/mul with toРёЋ and mod 6.
postulate
  _+6_ : Z6 Рєњ Z6 Рєњ Z6
  _*6_ : Z6 Рєњ Z6 Рєњ Z6

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- von Neumann regular inverse witness: a = a*b*a

Regular : Z6 Рєњ Set
Regular a = ╬Б Z6 (╬╗ b Рєњ a РЅА (a *6 b) *6 a)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete witness table (finite, so we can just provide b per a).
-- You can later refine _+6_/_*6_ and this becomes fully checkable.

postulate
  bOf : Z6 Рєњ Z6
  regular-law : Рѕђ a Рєњ a РЅА (a *6 bOf a) *6 a

regular : Рѕђ a Рєњ Regular a
regular a = bOf a , regular-law a
module FascisticSystem where

open import Data.Product using (╬Б; _,_)
open import Data.Sum using (_Ріј_; injРѓЂ; injРѓѓ)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_РЅА_)

open import Data.Nat as Nat
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)



-- Abstract finite state space

postulate
  S : Set
  finiteS : РёЋ          -- cardinality (not constructively used)

-- Entropy function (measure into РёЋ for simplicity)

postulate
  H : S Рєњ РёЋ

-- Projection operator (idempotent, non-invertible)

record Projection : Set where
  field
    K        : S Рєњ S
    idemp    : Рѕђ s Рєњ K (K s) РЅА K s
    contract : Рѕђ s Рєњ H (K s) РЅц H s

-- System = list of projections applied in fixed order

postulate
  Ktotal : S Рєњ S

-- Global contraction property

postulate
  monotone : Рѕђ s Рєњ H (Ktotal s) РЅц H s

-- Strict decrease when not in fixed set

postulate
  strict-decrease :
    Рѕђ s Рєњ H (Ktotal s) < H s Ріј (Ktotal s РЅА s)

-- Define attractor

Attractor : Set
Attractor = ╬Б S (╬╗ s Рєњ Ktotal s РЅА s)

-- Iteration

iterate : РёЋ Рєњ S Рєњ S
iterate zero    s = s
iterate (suc n) s = Ktotal (iterate n s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- РђюAxiom of completionРђЮ as a termination measure contract:
-- Completion prime provides a stop condition for any recursive refinement loop.

record CompletionLaw (S : Set) : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    measure : S Рєњ Nat
    step    : S Рєњ S
    -- If step decreases measure, recursion terminates.
    decreases : Рѕђ s Рєњ measure (step s) < measure s
module ThreeAdic_Attractor where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Data.Rational using (Рёџ; _+_; _-_; _*_; _/_; normalize)
open import Data.Rational.Properties as РёџP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Define x by the equation 3x = x - 1, and solve in Рёџ.
-- This is the algebraic Рђюdigit-shiftРђЮ property you care about.

postulate
  x : Рёџ

-- Helpers (stdlib has numerals; we keep explicit)
postulate
  1Рёџ : Рёџ
  2Рёџ : Рёџ
  3Рёџ : Рёџ
  minusHalfQ : Рёџ

postulate
  shift : (3Рёџ * x) РЅА (x - 1Рёџ)
  qed : x РЅА minusHalfQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Theorem: if 3x = x - 1 then x = -1/2

solve : shift РЅА shift Рєњ x РЅА minusHalfQ
solve _ =
  -- You can fill this using Рёџ ring reasoning:
  -- 3x = x - 1  РЄњ  2x = -1  РЄњ x = -1/2
  -- In Agda, easiest is to use РёџP.*-cancel╩│ / group properties.
  qed
module MonsterState where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_РЅА_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _Рѕи_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Factor mask (15 prime-power factors of |M|).
-- true  = keep
-- false = remove

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

Mask : Set
Mask = List Bool

replicate : Nat Рєњ Bool Рєњ Mask
replicate zero    b = []
replicate (suc n) b = b Рѕи replicate n b

fullMask : Mask
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

emptyMask : Mask
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Walk state.
-- You can extend this with Рђюwindow positionРђЮ, Рђюtarget digitsРђЮ, etc.
-- For DASHI: kernel is about how masks evolve; lens decides admissibility.

record State : Set where
  constructor st
  field
    mask   : Mask
    window : Nat   -- abstract Рђюdigit window idРђЮ (moving window, index, etc.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A lens is the measurement predicate:
-- admissible s m = Рђюremoving to mask m preserves the digit window conditionРђЮ.

record Lens : SetРѓЂ where
  field
    admissible : State Рєњ Mask Рєњ Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Candidate moves:
-- In the real system, this is Рђюremove subsets of prime-power factorsРђЮ.
-- Here we just take a finite list of candidate masks.

Candidates : Set
Candidates = List Mask
module LogicTlurey where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Local equality utilities (no stdlib needed)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

sym : Рѕђ {A : Set} {x y : A} Рєњ x РЅА y Рєњ y РЅА x
sym refl = refl

cong : Рѕђ {A B : Set} {x y : A} (f : A Рєњ B) Рєњ x РЅА y Рєњ f x РЅА f y
cong f refl = refl

open import Base369

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dialectical stages
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Stage : Set where
  seed      : Stage
  counter   : Stage
  resonance : Stage
  overflow  : Stage

next : Stage Рєњ Stage
next seed      = counter
next counter   = resonance
next resonance = overflow
next overflow  = seed

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tlurey traces
------------------------------------------------------------------------

StageTrace : Nat Рєњ Stage Рєњ List Stage
StageTrace zero    _ = []
StageTrace (suc n) s = s Рѕи StageTrace n (next s)

length : Рѕђ {A : Set} Рєњ List A Рєњ Nat
length []       = zero
length (_ Рѕи xs) = suc (length xs)

_++_ : Рѕђ {A : Set} Рєњ List A Рєњ List A Рєњ List A
[]       ++ ys = ys
(x Рѕи xs) ++ ys = x Рѕи (xs ++ ys)

StageTrace-length : Рѕђ n s Рєњ length (StageTrace n s) РЅА n
StageTrace-length zero    _ = refl
StageTrace-length (suc n) s = cong suc (StageTrace-length n (next s))

nextРЂ┤ : Рѕђ s Рєњ spin 4 next s РЅА s
nextРЂ┤ seed      = refl
nextРЂ┤ counter   = refl
nextРЂ┤ resonance = refl
nextРЂ┤ overflow  = refl

spin-next-succ : Рѕђ n s Рєњ spin n next (next s) РЅА spin (suc n) next s
spin-next-succ zero    _ = refl
spin-next-succ (suc n) s = cong next (spin-next-succ n s)

StageTrace-periodic : Рѕђ n s Рєњ StageTrace (n + 4) s РЅА StageTrace n s ++ StageTrace 4 (spin n next s)
StageTrace-periodic zero    s = refl
StageTrace-periodic (suc n) s rewrite sym (spin-next-succ n s) =
  cong (s Рѕи_) (StageTrace-periodic n (next s))

StageTrace-cycle : Рѕђ n Рєњ StageTrace (n + 4) seed РЅА StageTrace n seed ++ StageTrace 4 (spin n next seed)
StageTrace-cycle n = StageTrace-periodic n seed


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Semantics via triadic values
------------------------------------------------------------------------

stageTone : Stage Рєњ TriTruth
stageTone seed      = tri-low
stageTone counter   = tri-mid
stageTone resonance = tri-high
stageTone overflow  = tri-low

combineStage : Stage Рєњ Stage Рєњ TriTruth
combineStage a b = triXor (stageTone a) (stageTone b)

stageTone-next-seed : stageTone (next seed) РЅА rotateTri (stageTone seed)
stageTone-next-seed = refl

stageTone-next-counter : stageTone (next counter) РЅА rotateTri (stageTone counter)
stageTone-next-counter = refl

stageTone-next-resonance : stageTone (next resonance) РЅА rotateTri (stageTone resonance)
stageTone-next-resonance = refl

stageTone-next-overflow : stageTone (next overflow) РЅА stageTone seed
stageTone-next-overflow = refl

resonance-combine : combineStage resonance resonance РЅА tri-mid
resonance-combine = refl
module MonsterGroups where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _Рѕи_)

open import MonsterState

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Boundary predicate: Рђюthis state ends a groupРђЮ.
-- You define it from the walk semantics (or from the trace table markers).

Boundary : Set
Boundary = State Рєњ Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Count groups in a trace given a boundary predicate.
-- Convention: group count starts at 0 for empty trace, else 1 + boundaries hit.

countGroups : Boundary Рєњ List State Рєњ Nat
countGroups b [] = 0
countGroups b (s Рѕи ss) = suc (go ss)
  where
    go : List State Рєњ Nat
    go [] = 0
    go (t Рѕи ts) with b t
    ... | true  = suc (go ts)
    ... | false = go ts

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- You can similarly count Рђюpreserved digitsРђЮ if your trace stores that.
-- For now keep it abstract until you add a field.
-- Agda: 10-Fold Way Bridges
module TenfoldBridges where

open import Data.Nat using (РёЋ)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (_%_)
open import Data.Bool
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_РЅА_; refl; sym; _РЅб_)

-- Topological class
topoClass : РёЋ Рєњ РёЋ
topoClass n = n % 10

-- Bridge record
record Bridge : Set where
  field
    nodeA : РёЋ
    nodeB : РёЋ
    different : topoClass nodeA РЅб topoClass nodeB

-- Symmetry
bridge-sym : (b : Bridge) Рєњ Bridge
bridge-sym record { nodeA = a ; nodeB = b ; different = d } =
  record { nodeA = b ; nodeB = a ; different = ╬╗ eq Рєњ d (sym eq) }

-- Example: 232 Рєћ 323
bridge-232-323 : Bridge
bridge-232-323 = record
  { nodeA = 232
  ; nodeB = 323
  ; different = ╬╗ ()
  }

-- Theorem: Symmetry preserves bridges
bridge-symmetry : (b : Bridge) Рєњ 
  Bridge.nodeA (bridge-sym b) РЅА Bridge.nodeB b
bridge-symmetry b = refl
